function ensureHayUpgradeIconSlots()
	if type(AssetSlots) ~= "table" then
		AssetSlots = {}
	end
	if type(AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons) ~= "table" then
		AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons = {}
	end
	local icons = AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons
	icons["HayAmount"] = icons["HayAmount"] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayAmountUpgradeIcon or ""
	icons["HayMultiplier"] = icons["HayMultiplier"] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayMultiplierUpgradeIcon or ""
	icons["HayCooldown"] = icons["HayCooldown"] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayCooldownUpgradeIcon or ""
end
ensureHayUpgradeIconSlots()

	AssetSlots.PassiveIndexBackgrounds[passiveId] = ""
	AssetSlots.PassiveInventoryBackgrounds[passiveId] = ""
end

function getRuneBoardTheme(systemId)
	return RUNE_BOARD_THEMES[systemId or "Nature"] or RUNE_BOARD_THEMES.Nature
end

function getRuneVisual(runeId)
	return RUNE_VISUALS[runeId] or {name = tostring(runeId or "Rune"), chance = "?", baseDenominator = 1, rowColor = Color3.fromRGB(35, 55, 45), accent = Color3.fromRGB(165, 255, 120), icon = "◈", backgroundAsset = ""}
end

function getRuneIconAsset(runeId)
	local cfg = type(RUNE_ASSET_CONFIG[runeId]) == "table" and RUNE_ASSET_CONFIG[runeId] or {}
	return getAssetOrEmpty(cfg.iconAsset or AssetSlots.RuneIcons[runeId] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.RuneCommon)
end

function getRuneDetailBackgroundAsset(runeId)
	local cfg = type(RUNE_ASSET_CONFIG[runeId]) == "table" and RUNE_ASSET_CONFIG[runeId] or {}
	local visual = RUNE_VISUALS[runeId]
	return getAssetOrEmpty(cfg.detailBackgroundAsset or (visual and visual.backgroundAsset) or "")
end

function roundToTenth(value)
	return math.floor((tonumber(value) or 0) * 10 + 0.5) / 10
end

function formatNumber(value)
	value = tonumber(value) or 0
	local sign = value < 0 and "-" or ""
	local absValue = math.abs(value)
	local suffixes = {"", "K", "M", "B", "T", "Qa", "Qi", "Sx", "SP", "OC", "NO"}

	if absValue < 1000 then
		if absValue % 1 == 0 then
			return sign .. tostring(math.floor(absValue))
		end
		local exact = string.format("%.2f", absValue)
		exact = exact:gsub("(%..-)0+$", "%1"):gsub("%.$", "")
		return sign .. exact
	end

	local idx = 1
	while absValue >= 1000 and idx < #suffixes do
		absValue /= 1000
		idx += 1
	end
	local digits = absValue >= 100 and 0 or (absValue >= 10 and 1 or 2)
	local formatted = string.format("%." .. tostring(digits) .. "f", absValue)
	formatted = formatted:gsub("(%..-)0+$", "%1"):gsub("%.$", "")
	return sign .. formatted .. suffixes[idx]
end

function getPassiveBonusLines(def)
	local lines = {}
	function addMul(label, value)
		if tonumber(value) and math.abs((tonumber(value) or 1) - 1) > 0.0001 then
			table.insert(lines, string.format("• %s x%s", label, formatNumber(value)))
		end
	end
	function addAdd(label, value)
		if tonumber(value) and math.abs(tonumber(value)) > 0.0001 then
			table.insert(lines, string.format("• %s +%s", label, formatNumber(value)))
		end
	end
	addMul("Coins", def.coinMultiplier)
	addMul("Wood", def.woodMultiplier)
	addMul("Global", def.globalMultiplier)
	addMul("Speed", def.speedMultiplier)
	addMul("XP", def.xpMultiplier)
	addMul("Rune Luck", def.runeLuckMultiplier)
	addMul("Rune Speed", def.runeSpeedMultiplier)
	addMul("Rune Bulk", def.runeBulkMultiplier)
	addAdd("Rune Bulk", def.runeBulkAdd)
	if #lines == 0 then
		table.insert(lines, "• Без доп. бонусов")
	end
	return lines
end

function getAssetOrEmpty(assetId)
	if assetId and assetId ~= "" and not string.find(assetId, "PASTE") then
		return assetId
	end
	return ""
end


function safeClamp(value, minValue, maxValue)
	value = tonumber(value) or tonumber(minValue) or 0
	minValue = tonumber(minValue) or 0
	maxValue = tonumber(maxValue) or minValue

	if maxValue < minValue then
		maxValue = minValue
	end

	return math.clamp(value, minValue, maxValue)
end

function getDeviceType()
	local view = workspace.CurrentCamera and workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1920, 1080)
	local touch = UserInputService.TouchEnabled
	local keyboard = UserInputService.KeyboardEnabled
	local minAxis = math.min(view.X, view.Y)
	local maxAxis = math.max(view.X, view.Y)
	local ratio = maxAxis / math.max(1, minAxis)
	local insetTopLeft, insetBottomRight = GuiService:GetGuiInset()
	local insetHeight = math.abs(insetTopLeft.Y) + math.abs(insetBottomRight.Y)

	if touch and (not keyboard) and (minAxis <= 720 or ratio >= 1.78) then
		return "Phone"
	elseif touch and (minAxis <= 1100 or insetHeight > 0) then
		return "Tablet"
	end

	return "Laptop/Desktop"
end

function getDevicePreset()
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	local viewport = camera and camera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1920, 1080)
	local insetTopLeft, insetBottomRight = GuiService:GetGuiInset()
	local width = math.max(320, viewport.X - math.abs(insetTopLeft.X) - math.abs(insetBottomRight.X))
	local _touchEnabled = UserInputService.TouchEnabled
	local _keyboardEnabled = UserInputService.KeyboardEnabled

	if width < 800 then
		return "PHONE"
	elseif width < 1400 then
		return "TABLET_LAPTOP"
	else
		return "DESKTOP"
	end
end

function getDeviceProfile()
	local preset = getDevicePreset and getDevicePreset() or "DESKTOP"
	if preset == "PHONE" then
		return "mobile"
	elseif preset == "TABLET_LAPTOP" or preset == "LAPTOP_TABLET" then
		return "tablet"
	end
	return "desktop"
end

DEVICE_GUI_PRESETS = {
	PHONE = {scaleMin = 0.72, scaleMax = 0.88, scaleBase = 980, panelPadX = 28, panelPadY = 40, scrollBar = 16, cardWidth = 196, buttonHeight = 36, textSize = 14},
	TABLET_LAPTOP = {scaleMin = 0.88, scaleMax = 1.0, scaleBase = 1050, panelPadX = 32, panelPadY = 40, scrollBar = 14, cardWidth = 246, buttonHeight = 34, textSize = 15},
	DESKTOP = {scaleMin = 1, scaleMax = 1, scaleBase = 1080, panelPadX = 48, panelPadY = 56, scrollBar = 12, cardWidth = 262, buttonHeight = 36, textSize = 16},
}
DEVICE_GUI_PRESETS.LAPTOP_TABLET = DEVICE_GUI_PRESETS.TABLET_LAPTOP

function getGuiPreset()
	local deviceConfig = DEVICE_GUI_PRESETS[getDevicePreset()]
	if not deviceConfig then
		warn("deviceConfig nil")
		return DEVICE_GUI_PRESETS.DESKTOP
	end
	return deviceConfig
end

function createCorner(parent, radius)
	local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
	corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, radius or 12)
	corner.Parent = parent
	return corner
end

function createStroke(parent, color, thickness, transparency)
	local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	stroke.Color = color or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	stroke.Thickness = thickness or 1
	stroke.Transparency = transparency or 0
	stroke.Parent = parent
	return stroke
end

function createGradient(parent, color1, color2, rotation)
	local gradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	gradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, color1),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, color2),
	})
	gradient.Rotation = rotation or 90
	gradient.Parent = parent
	return gradient
end

function addScaleHover(button)
	local scale = Instance.new("UIScale")
	scale.Scale = 1
	scale.Parent = button

	button.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
		TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Scale = 1.05}):Play()
	end)

	button.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
		TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Scale = 1}):Play()
	end)

	if button:IsA("GuiButton") then
		button.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
			TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {Scale = 0.96}):Play()
		end)

		button.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
			TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {Scale = 1.05}):Play()
		end)
	end
end

function animatePanelVisibility(panel, visible)
	if not panel then return end
	local scale = panel:FindFirstChild("PanelMotionScale")
	if not scale then
		scale = Instance.new("UIScale")
		scale.Name = "PanelMotionScale"
		scale.Scale = 1
		scale.Parent = panel
	end
	if visible then
		panel.Visible = true
		panel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		scale.Scale = 0.94
		TweenService:Create(panel, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
		TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.22, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Scale = 1}):Play()
	else
		local tw = TweenService:Create(panel, TweenInfo.new(0.14, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {BackgroundTransparency = 1})
		TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.14, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Scale = 0.96}):Play()
		tw:Play()
		tw.Completed:Connect(function() panel.Visible = false panel.BackgroundTransparency = 0 scale.Scale = 1 end)
	end
end

function pulseStroke(stroke, lowTransparency, highTransparency, seconds)
	if not stroke then return end
	TweenService:Create(stroke, TweenInfo.new(seconds or 1.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		Transparency = highTransparency or 0.35,
	}):Play()
	stroke.Transparency = lowTransparency or stroke.Transparency
end

function inferUpgradeSystem(titleText)
	local text = tostring(titleText or "")
	if string.find(text, "Hay") then return "Hay" end
	if string.find(text, "XP") then return "XP" end
	if string.find(text, "Paper") then return "Paper" end
	if string.find(text, "Wood") or string.find(text, "Tree") then return "Wood" end
	if string.find(text, "Rebirth") then return "Rebirth" end
	if string.find(text, "Passive") then return "Passive" end
	if string.find(text, "Rune") then return "Rune" end
	if string.find(text, "Coin") or string.find(text, "Spawn") then return "Coin" end
	return "Rune"
end

function getUpgradeTheme(systemName)
	local themes = type(UPGRADE_CARD_THEMES) == "table" and UPGRADE_CARD_THEMES or {}
	return themes[systemName or "Rune"] or themes.Rune or themes.Coin or {
		card1 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 48, 62), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 22, 30), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(54, 64, 84), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 28, 38), header1 = Color3.fromRGB(96, 128, 190), header2 = Color3.fromRGB(48, 62, 100), stroke = Color3.fromRGB(180, 210, 255), text = Color3.fromRGB(244, 248, 255), subtext = Color3.fromRGB(210, 220, 240), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 210, 255), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 130, 220), badge1 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 210, 255), badge2 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 115, 190), badgeText = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), btn1 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 190, 255), btn2 = Color3.fromRGB(74, 130, 225), btnMax1 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 180, 255), btnMax2 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 100, 220), btnText = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), glow = Color3.fromRGB(150, 190, 255), currency = ""
	}
end

function mergeUpgradeTheme(systemName, overrides)
	local safeSystem = tostring(systemName or "Rune")
	local base = getUpgradeTheme(safeSystem)
	local merged = {}
	if type(base) == "table" then
		for k, v in pairs(base) do merged[k] = v end
	end
	if type(overrides) == "table" then
		for k, v in pairs(overrides) do merged[k] = v end
	end
	merged["system"] = safeSystem
	return merged
end

function getUpgradeSystemFromPalette(palette, titleText)
	if type(palette) == "table" and type(rawget(palette, "system")) == "string" and rawget(palette, "system") ~= "" then
		return rawget(palette, "system")
	end
	return inferUpgradeSystem(titleText)
end

function pulseStroke(stroke, lowTransparency, highTransparency, seconds)
	if not stroke then return end
	TweenService:Create(stroke, TweenInfo.new(seconds or 1.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		Transparency = highTransparency or 0.35,
	}):Play()
	stroke.Transparency = lowTransparency or stroke.Transparency
end

function createDecorDots(parent, count)
	for _ = 1, count do
		local dot = Instance.new("Frame")
		dot.Size = UDim2.new(0, math.random(8, 26), 0, math.random(8, 26))
		dot.Position = UDim2.new(math.random(), -10, math.random(), -10)
		dot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		dot.BackgroundTransparency = 0.92
		dot.BorderSizePixel = 0
		dot.Parent = parent
		createCorner(dot, 999)
	end
end

function createWorldBoard(name, adorneePart, face, pixelsPerStud)
	local old = playerGui:FindFirstChild(name)
	if old then
		old:Destroy()
	end

	local surfaceGui = Instance.new("SurfaceGui")
	surfaceGui.Name = name
	surfaceGui.Adornee = adorneePart
	surfaceGui.Face = face or Enum.NormalId.Front
	surfaceGui.AlwaysOnTop = true
	surfaceGui.LightInfluence = 0
	surfaceGui.Brightness = 2
	surfaceGui.MaxDistance = 80
	surfaceGui.PixelsPerStud = pixelsPerStud or 80
	surfaceGui.SizingMode = Enum.SurfaceGuiSizingMode.PixelsPerStud
	surfaceGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
	surfaceGui.Parent = playerGui

	local BOARD_THEMES = {
		Coins = {a=Color3.fromRGB(124,82,18), b=Color3.fromRGB(64,39,7), s=Color3.fromRGB(255,222,94)},
		Tree = {a=Color3.fromRGB(54,92,44), b=Color3.fromRGB(69,43,19), s=Color3.fromRGB(154,225,116)},
		Paper = {a=Color3.fromRGB(232,238,246), b=Color3.fromRGB(174,192,214), s=Color3.fromRGB(151,205,255)},
		Rune = {a=Color3.fromRGB(30,78,40), b=Color3.fromRGB(8,22,18), s=Color3.fromRGB(160,255,88)},
		ForestRune = {a=Color3.fromRGB(42,67,32), b=Color3.fromRGB(45,27,13), s=Color3.fromRGB(135,224,111)},
		NatureRune = {a=Color3.fromRGB(42,142,48), b=Color3.fromRGB(8,46,18), s=Color3.fromRGB(125,255,132)},
		XP = {a=Color3.fromRGB(45,74,150), b=Color3.fromRGB(58,35,120), s=Color3.fromRGB(144,178,255)},
		Hay = {a=Color3.fromRGB(154,113,30), b=Color3.fromRGB(96,61,12), s=Color3.fromRGB(255,226,126)},
		Rebirth = {a=Color3.fromRGB(106,45,128), b=Color3.fromRGB(47,18,74), s=Color3.fromRGB(255,153,236)},
		Passive = {a=Color3.fromRGB(46,50,72), b=Color3.fromRGB(18,21,34), s=Color3.fromRGB(202,174,255)},
	}
	local theme = BOARD_THEMES.Rune
	if string.find(name, "Coin") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Coins
	elseif string.find(name, "Tree") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Tree
	elseif string.find(name, "Paper") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Paper
	elseif string.find(name, "ForestRune") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.ForestRune
	elseif string.find(name, "NatureRune") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.NatureRune
	elseif string.find(name, "XP") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.XP
	elseif string.find(name, "Hay") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Hay
	elseif string.find(name, "Rebirth") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Rebirth
	elseif string.find(name, "Passive") then theme = BOARD_THEMES.Passive
	end

	local root = Instance.new("Frame")
	root.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	root.BackgroundColor3 = theme.a
	root.BorderSizePixel = 0
	root.Parent = surfaceGui
	createGradient(root, theme.a, theme.b, 90)
	createStroke(root, theme.s, 2, 0.08)
	createDecorDots(root, 10)
	for i = 1, 4 do
		local band = Instance.new("Frame")
		band.Size = UDim2.new(1.15, 0, 0, 10 + i * 3)
		band.Position = UDim2.new(-0.08, 0, 0.12 * i, 0)
		band.Rotation = -8 + i * 3
		band.BackgroundColor3 = theme.s
		band.BackgroundTransparency = 0.88
		band.BorderSizePixel = 0
		band.Parent = root
		createCorner(band, 999)
	end

	local inner = Instance.new("Frame")
	inner.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, -12)
	inner.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6)
	inner.BackgroundColor3 = theme.b
	inner.BorderSizePixel = 0
	inner.Parent = root
	createCorner(inner, 18)
	createGradient(inner, theme.a, theme.b, 90)
	createStroke(inner, theme.s, 1.4, 0.12)

	local content = Instance.new("Frame")
	content.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 1, -16)
	content.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 8)
	content.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	content.Parent = inner

	return surfaceGui, content
end

	title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	title.TextScaled = true
	title.Parent = header

	local subtitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	subtitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	subtitle.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 18)
	subtitle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 32)
	subtitle.Text = subtitleText
	subtitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 235, 170)
	subtitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	subtitle.TextScaled = true

	local line = Instance.new("Frame")

	line.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 255, 110)
	line.BackgroundTransparency = 0.18
	line.BorderSizePixel = 0
	line.Parent = header
end

local function applyResponsiveScale(targetGui)
	local scale = Instance.new("UIScale")
	scale.Scale = 1
	scale.Parent = targetGui
	local function refresh()
		local view = workspace.CurrentCamera and workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1920,1080)
		local minAxis = math.max(640, math.min(view.X, view.Y))
		local presetName = getDevicePreset()
		local preset = getGuiPreset()
		if presetName == "DESKTOP" then
			scale.Scale = 1
		else
			scale.Scale = safeClamp(minAxis / preset.scaleBase, preset.scaleMin, preset.scaleMax)
		end
	end
	refresh()
	if workspace.CurrentCamera then
		workspace.CurrentCamera:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ViewportSize"):Connect(refresh)
	end
end

applyResponsiveScale(screenGui)

local function applyResponsivePanel(panel, ratioX, ratioY, maxWidth, maxHeight, position)
	local function refresh()
		local view = workspace.CurrentCamera and workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1920, 1080)
		local insetTopLeft, insetBottomRight = GuiService:GetGuiInset()
		local safeWidth = math.max(320, view.X - math.abs(insetTopLeft.X) - math.abs(insetBottomRight.X))
		local safeHeight = math.max(320, view.Y - math.abs(insetTopLeft.Y) - math.abs(insetBottomRight.Y))
		local profile = getDeviceProfile()
		local widthMax = maxWidth or 900
		local heightMax = maxHeight or 620
		local preset = getGuiPreset()
		local compactWidePanel = panel:GetAttribute("CompactWidePanel") == true
		local effectiveRatioX = ratioX or 0.7
		if profile == "mobile" then
			if compactWidePanel then
				effectiveRatioX = math.min(0.92, effectiveRatioX * 1.14)
				widthMax = widthMax * 1.12
			end
			widthMax = math.floor(math.min(safeWidth - preset.panelPadX, widthMax * 0.9))
			heightMax = math.floor(math.min(safeHeight - preset.panelPadY, heightMax * (compactWidePanel and 0.98 or 0.9)))
		elseif profile == "tablet" then
			if compactWidePanel then
				effectiveRatioX = math.min(0.9, effectiveRatioX * 1.12)
				widthMax = widthMax * 1.12
			end
			widthMax = math.floor(math.min(safeWidth - preset.panelPadX, widthMax * 0.98))
			heightMax = math.floor(math.min(safeHeight - preset.panelPadY, heightMax * 0.94))
		end
		local widthMin = profile == "mobile" and math.min(320, widthMax) or math.min(460, widthMax)
		local heightMin = profile == "mobile" and math.min(420, heightMax) or math.min(320, heightMax)
		local w = math.floor(safeClamp(safeWidth * effectiveRatioX, widthMin, widthMax))
		local h = math.floor(safeClamp(safeHeight * (ratioY or 0.7), heightMin, heightMax))
		panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, w, 0, h)
		if position then
			panel.Position = position
		end
	end
	refresh()
	if workspace.CurrentCamera then
		workspace.CurrentCamera:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ViewportSize"):Connect(refresh)
	end
end

function refreshAdminPanelForDevice()
	local preset = getDevicePreset()
	local compact = preset == "PHONE"
	local tablet = preset == "TABLET_LAPTOP" or preset == "LAPTOP_TABLET"
	if compact then
		adminFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 228, 0, 286)
		adminFrame.Position = UDim2.new(1, -6, 0, 6)
		if adminPadding then
			adminPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 8)
			adminPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 8)
			adminPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 8)
			adminPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 8)
		end
		if adminTitle then adminTitle.TextSize = 14 end
		adminEventGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 188, 0, 82)
		adminEventLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 3)
	elseif tablet then
		adminFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 286, 0, 352)
		adminFrame.Position = UDim2.new(1, -14, 0, 14)
		if adminPadding then
			adminPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 10)
			adminPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 10)
			adminPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
			adminPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 10)
		end
		if adminTitle then adminTitle.TextSize = 17 end
		adminEventGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 230, 0, 102)
		adminEventLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 5)
	else
		adminFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 320, 0, 390)
		adminFrame.Position = UDim2.new(1, -18, 0, 18)
		if adminPadding then
			adminPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 12)
			adminPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 12)
			adminPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 12)
			adminPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 12)
		end
		if adminTitle then adminTitle.TextSize = 20 end
		adminEventGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 250, 0, 110)
		adminEventLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 6)
	end

	if not (compact or tablet) then
		return
	end

	local buttonHeight = compact and 24 or 28
	local textSize = compact and 11 or 13
	if adminTabs then
		adminTabs.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, compact and 24 or 32)
	end
	for _, button in ipairs({tabCurrency, tabPersonal, tabEvents, giveCurrencyButton, resetButton, givePassiveButton, adminRuneBoostButton, startAllEventsButton, duration5Button, duration15Button, duration60Button}) do
		if button then
			button.TextScaled = false
			button.TextSize = textSize
		end
	end
	if adminAmountBox then
		adminAmountBox.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, compact and 28 or 36)
		adminAmountBox.TextSize = textSize
	end
	if currencySelector then
		currencySelector.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, compact and 36 or 46)
		currencySelector.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, compact and 26 or 34)
	end
	if giveCurrencyButton then
		giveCurrencyButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, compact and 68 or 86)
		giveCurrencyButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, buttonHeight)
	end
	if resetButton then
		resetButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, compact and 98 or 126)
		resetButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, buttonHeight)
	end
	for _, quickButton in ipairs(adminQuickButtons or {}) do
		quickButton.Position = UDim2.new(quickButton.Position.X.Scale, 0, 0, compact and 128 or 166)
		quickButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.31, 0, 0, compact and 20 or 24)
		quickButton.TextScaled = false
		quickButton.TextSize = compact and 10 or 12
	end
	if adminCoinChainLabel then
		adminCoinChainLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, compact and 154 or 196)
		adminCoinChainLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, compact and 34 or 44)
		adminCoinChainLabel.TextSize = compact and 9 or 11
	end
	for _, eventButton in pairs(eventButtons or {}) do
		eventButton.TextScaled = false
		eventButton.TextSize = compact and 10 or 12
		eventButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, compact and 22 or 26)
	end
end

adminQuickButtons = {}
function createAdminQuickCurrencyButton(text, amount, xScale)
	local b = Instance.new("TextButton")
	b.Position = UDim2.new(xScale, 0, 0, 166)
	b.Size = UDim2.new(0.31, 0, 0, 24)
	b.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(132, 176, 255)
	b.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 38, 64)
	b.Text = text
	b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	b.TextScaled = true
	b.Parent = adminSectionCurrency
	b.BorderSizePixel = 0
	b:SetAttribute("Amount", amount)
	createCorner(b, 9)
	addScaleHover(b)
	table.insert(adminQuickButtons, b)
	return b
end

local function mkGamepassButton(y, text, key)
	local b = Instance.new("TextButton")
	b.Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,y)
	b.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,27)
	b.Text = text
	b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold

	b.Parent = adminGamepassSection
	b.BorderSizePixel = 0
	createCorner(b,9)
	b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		local owns, status = checkGamepassOwnership(key)
		syncGamepassValue(key, owns)
		showToast(text .. ": " .. status)
		if updateBoards then updateBoards() end
	end)
end

function refreshAdminCurrencyButtons()
	if selectedAdminCurrency == "Coins" then
		selectCoinsButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 206, 80)
		selectCoinsButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 42, 56)
		selectWoodButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
		selectWoodButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
		selectPaperButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
		selectPaperButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
		selectXPButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
		selectXPButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
	else
		selectCoinsButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
		selectCoinsButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
		if selectedAdminCurrency == "Wood" then
			selectWoodButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(130, 160, 120)
			selectWoodButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			selectPaperButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
			selectPaperButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
			selectXPButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
			selectXPButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
		else
			if selectedAdminCurrency == "Paper" then
				selectWoodButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
				selectWoodButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
				selectPaperButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(206, 216, 240)
				selectPaperButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 56, 77)
				selectXPButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
				selectXPButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
			else
				selectWoodButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
				selectWoodButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
				selectPaperButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 110, 125)
				selectPaperButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
				selectXPButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 196, 255)
				selectXPButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 50, 70)
			end
		end
	end
end

function createStatRow(parent, titleText)
	local row = Instance.new("Frame")
	row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 38)
	row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 26, 18)
	row.BorderSizePixel = 0
	row.Parent = parent
	createCorner(row, 10)
	createGradient(row, Color3.fromRGB(26, 38, 28), Color3.fromRGB(10, 18, 12), 0)
	createStroke(row, Color3.fromRGB(142, 255, 108), 1.2, 0.08)

	local marker = Instance.new("Frame")
	marker.Size = UDim2.new(0, 8, 1, -12)
	marker.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6)
	marker.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(148, 255, 105)
	marker.BorderSizePixel = 0
	marker.Parent = row
	createCorner(marker, 6)
	createGradient(marker, Color3.fromRGB(184, 255, 140), Color3.fromRGB(102, 255, 118), 90)

	local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	title.Size = UDim2.new(0.58, 0, 1, 0)
	title.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 0)
	title.Text = titleText
	title.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 255, 200)
	title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	title.TextScaled = true
	title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	title.Parent = row

	local value = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	value.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	value.Size = UDim2.new(0.34, -8, 1, 0)
	value.Position = UDim2.new(0.62, 0, 0, 0)
	value.Text = "-"
	value.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(236, 255, 228)
	value.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	value.TextScaled = true
	value.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
	value.Parent = row

	return value
end

function createIcon(parent, imageId, fallbackText, bg1, bg2)
	local holder = Instance.new("Frame")
	holder.Size = UDim2.new(0, 68, 0, 68)
	holder.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 24, 16)
	holder.BorderSizePixel = 0
	holder.Parent = parent
	createCorner(holder, 14)
	createGradient(holder, Color3.fromRGB(26, 40, 28), Color3.fromRGB(11, 18, 12), 45)
	createStroke(holder, Color3.fromRGB(151, 255, 116), 1.4, 0.08)

	local diamond = Instance.new("Frame")
	diamond.Size = UDim2.new(0, 48, 0, 48)
	diamond.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -24, 0.5, -24)
	diamond.BackgroundColor3 = bg1
	diamond.BorderSizePixel = 0
	diamond.Rotation = 45
	diamond.Parent = holder
	createCorner(diamond, 8)
	createGradient(diamond, bg1, bg2, 90)
	createStroke(diamond, Color3.fromRGB(212, 255, 194), 1.2, 0.15)

	local image = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	image.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, -20)
	image.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
	image.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	image.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
	image.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(imageId)
	image.Parent = holder

	local fallback = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	fallback.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	fallback.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	fallback.Text = fallbackText
	fallback.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	fallback.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	fallback.TextScaled = true
	fallback.Parent = holder

	if image.Image ~= "" then
		fallback.Visible = false
	else
		image.Visible = false
	end

	local scale = Instance.new("UIScale")
	scale.Scale = 1
	scale.Parent = holder

	TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(1.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		Scale = 1.06
	}):Play()

	return holder
end

function createUpgradeCard(parent, titleText, descriptionText, bonusText, iconImageId, fallbackText, palette)
	if not parent then
		return nil
	end
	local originalPalette = type(palette) == "table" and palette or nil
	local systemName = getUpgradeSystemFromPalette(originalPalette, titleText)
	palette = mergeUpgradeTheme(systemName, originalPalette)
	local compactTitle = tostring(titleText or "Upgrade")
	if compactTitle == "Coin Multiplier" then compactTitle = "Coin Multi" end
	if compactTitle == "Spawn Booster" or compactTitle == "Spawn Speed" then compactTitle = "Spawn" end
	if compactTitle == "Rune Multiplier" then compactTitle = "Rune Multi" end
	local card = Instance.new("Frame")
	local preset = getGuiPreset()
	card.Size = UDim2.new(0, palette.cardWidth or preset.cardWidth or 262, 1, -10)
	card.BackgroundColor3 = palette.card2
	card.BorderSizePixel = 0
	card.Parent = parent
	createCorner(card, 18)
	createGradient(card, palette.card1, palette.card2, 90)
	local outerStroke = createStroke(card, palette.glow or palette.stroke, 2.4, 0.06)
	pulseStroke(outerStroke, 0.06, 0.28, 1.8)
	addScaleHover(card)

	local glow = Instance.new("Frame")
	glow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 16, 1, 16)
	glow.Position = UDim2.new(0, -8, 0, -8)
	glow.BackgroundColor3 = palette.glow or palette.stroke
	glow.BackgroundTransparency = 0.88
	glow.BorderSizePixel = 0
	glow.ZIndex = math.max(0, card.ZIndex - 1)
	glow.Parent = card
	createCorner(glow, 22)

	local inner = Instance.new("Frame")
	inner.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, -12)
	inner.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6)
	inner.BackgroundColor3 = palette.inner2
	inner.BorderSizePixel = 0
	inner.Parent = card
	createCorner(inner, 16)
	createGradient(inner, palette.inner1, palette.inner2, 90)
	createStroke(inner, palette.stroke, 1.3, 0.16)

	local topHeader = Instance.new("Frame")
	topHeader.Size = UDim2.new(1, -14, 0, 54)
	topHeader.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 7)
	topHeader.BackgroundColor3 = palette.header2 or palette.inner1
	topHeader.BorderSizePixel = 0
	topHeader.Parent = inner
	createCorner(topHeader, 13)
	createGradient(topHeader, palette.header1 or palette.inner1, palette.header2 or palette.inner2, 0)
	createStroke(topHeader, palette.stroke, 1, 0.22)

	local icon = createIcon(topHeader, iconImageId, fallbackText, palette.icon1, palette.icon2)
	icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
	icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -18)

	local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	title.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 0, 21)
	title.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 6)
	title.Text = compactTitle
	title.TextColor3 = palette.text
	title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	title.TextScaled = true
	title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	title.Parent = topHeader

	local levelPill = Instance.new("Frame")
	levelPill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 74, 0, 19)
	levelPill.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)

		desc.TextScaled = false

		statusLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center

		maxButton.TextScaled = false
		maxButton.TextSize = 13
	end

	return {
		card = card,

end

function createLockedOverlay(parent, text)
	local overlay = Instance.new("Frame")
	overlay.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	overlay.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 24, 37)
	overlay.BackgroundTransparency = 0.18
	overlay.BorderSizePixel = 0
	overlay.Parent = parent
	createCorner(overlay, 18)
	createStroke(overlay, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), 2, 0.18)

	local icon = createIcon(overlay, ICON_ASSET_IDS.CurrencyTree, "?", Color3.fromRGB(171, 123, 76), Color3.fromRGB(108, 73, 44))
	icon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -34, 0.28, -34)

	local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 70)
	label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -15)
	label.Text = text
	label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(246, 250, 255)
	label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	label.TextWrapped = true
	label.TextScaled = true
	label.Parent = overlay

	return overlay
end

function createHorizontalScroller(parent, positionY, height)
	local scrolling = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
	scrolling.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, positionY)
	scrolling.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -positionY - height)
	scrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	scrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 12
	scrolling.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(170, 194, 255)
	scrolling.ScrollBarImageTransparency = 1
	scrolling.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 22, 38)
	scrolling.BackgroundTransparency = 0.25
	scrolling.BorderSizePixel = 0
	scrolling.ScrollingDirection = Enum.ScrollingDirection.X
	scrolling.ElasticBehavior = Enum.ElasticBehavior.WhenScrollable
	scrolling.ScrollingEnabled = true
	scrolling.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X
	scrolling.HorizontalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always
	scrolling.VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always
	scrolling.Parent = parent

	local layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
	layout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
	layout.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Left
	layout.VerticalAlignment = Enum.VerticalAlignment.Center
	layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 12)
	layout.Parent = scrolling

	local padding = Instance.new("UIPadding")
	padding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 6)
	padding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 6)
	padding.Parent = scrolling

	local function refreshScrollerForDevice()
		local profile = getDeviceProfile()
		if profile == "mobile" then
			scrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 20
			layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 16)
			padding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 12)
			padding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 12)
		elseif profile == "tablet" then
			scrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 18
			layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 14)
		else
			scrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 16
			layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 12)
		end
	end
	refreshScrollerForDevice()
	if workspace.CurrentCamera then
		workspace.CurrentCamera:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ViewportSize"):Connect(refreshScrollerForDevice)
	end

	function updateCanvas()
		scrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, layout.AbsoluteContentSize.X + 60, 0, 0)
	end

	layout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)
	updateCanvas()
	applyFreeScroll(scrolling, {minCanvasX = 340, minCanvasY = 140})

	return scrolling
end

function applyFreeScroll(scrollingFrame, opts)
	if not scrollingFrame or not scrollingFrame:IsA("ScrollingFrame") then return end
	opts = opts or {}
	scrollingFrame.ElasticBehavior = Enum.ElasticBehavior.Always
	scrollingFrame.ScrollBarImageTransparency = 1
	scrollingFrame.ScrollingEnabled = true
	scrollingFrame.VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always
	scrollingFrame.HorizontalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.Always
	scrollingFrame.ScrollBarThickness = math.max(scrollingFrame.ScrollBarThickness, tonumber(opts.thickness) or 14)
	local minX = tonumber(opts.minCanvasX) or 140
	local minY = tonumber(opts.minCanvasY) or 220
	local existing = scrollingFrame.CanvasSize
	scrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(existing.X.Scale, math.max(minX, existing.X.Offset), existing.Y.Scale, math.max(minY, existing.Y.Offset))
end

function createPaperUpgradeUi()
	if not paperUpgradeDoska then
		return nil, nil
	end

	local _, paperUpgradeBoard = createWorldBoard("PaperUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", paperUpgradeDoska, Enum.NormalId.Front, 78)
	createHeader(paperUpgradeBoard, "PAPER UPGRADES", "Буст производства бумаги")
	local paperScroll = createHorizontalScroller(paperUpgradeBoard, 66, 12)

	local paperGainCard = createUpgradeCard(paperScroll, "Paper Gain", "+1 бумаги за цикл.", "+1", AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons.PaperGain, "P", {
		system = "Paper",
		card1 = Color3.fromRGB(115, 172, 232), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(84, 121, 189), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(152, 203, 255), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(107, 151, 221), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(228, 239, 255), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(190, 214, 255),
	})
	local paperMultiCard = createUpgradeCard(paperScroll, "Paper Multi", "+0.1x к производству.", "+0.1x", AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons.PaperMultiplier, "x", {
		system = "Paper",
		card1 = Color3.fromRGB(171, 140, 238), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(118, 92, 184), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(212, 188, 255), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(154, 126, 227), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 171, 223), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(198, 136, 255),
	})
	local paperSpeedCard = createUpgradeCard(paperScroll, "Paper Speed", "-0.5с цикла (до 10).", "-0.5s", AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons.PaperSpeed, "S", {
		system = "Paper",
		card1 = Color3.fromRGB(114, 218, 186), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(77, 173, 141), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(157, 240, 214), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(104, 198, 168), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(122, 226, 255), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(108, 158, 255),
	})

	local cards = {gain = paperGainCard, multi = paperMultiCard, speed = paperSpeedCard}
	local lockedOverlay = createLockedOverlay(paperUpgradeBoard, "Откроется на 4-м перерождении")
	return cards, lockedOverlay
end

	Grass = {per = "+0.10x Coins", base = 0.10, cap = 2.5, target = "Coins"},
	DarkGrass = {per = "+0.25x Coins", base = 0.25, cap = 15, target = "Coins"},

	Poleno = {per = "+0.10x Paper, +0.10x Wood", base = 0.10, cap = 5, target = "Paper/Wood"},
	ObgorevshiyPen = {per = "+0.10x Passive Luck", base = 0.10, cap = 3, target = "Passive Luck"},

function createRuneIndexBoard(runeSystemConfig)
	if not runeSystemConfig or not runeSystemConfig["id"] then
		warn("Rune index board skipped: missing rune system config")
		return nil
	end
	if not runeSystemConfig.partIndex then return nil end
	local theme = getRuneBoardTheme(runeSystemConfig["id"])
	local _, board = createWorldBoard(runeSystemConfig.indexGuiName, runeSystemConfig.partIndex, Enum.NormalId.Front, 72)
	if not board then return nil end
	createHeader(board, runeSystemConfig["id"] .. " RUNE INDEX", "Выбери руну для деталей")
	local list = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
	list.Size = UDim2.new(0.42, 0, 1, -68)
	list.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 66)
	list.BackgroundColor3 = theme.root2
	list.BackgroundTransparency = 0.08
	list.BorderSizePixel = 0
	list.ScrollBarThickness = getGuiPreset().scrollBar
	list.ScrollBarImageColor3 = theme.accent
	list.ElasticBehavior = Enum.ElasticBehavior.WhenScrollable
	list.Parent = board
	applyFreeScroll(list, {minCanvasY = 420})
	createCorner(list, 12)
	createStroke(list, theme.accent, 1.3, 0.18)
	createGradient(list, theme.root1, theme.root2, 90)
	local layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
	layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 4 or 6)
	layout.Parent = list
	layout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
		list.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, layout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 8)
	end)

	local details = Instance.new("Frame")
	details.Size = UDim2.new(0.58, -8, 1, -68)
	details.Position = UDim2.new(0.42, 8, 0, 66)
	details.BackgroundColor3 = theme.detail2
	details.BorderSizePixel = 0
	details.Parent = board
	createCorner(details, 12)
	createStroke(details, theme.accent, 1.6, 0.12)
	createGradient(details, theme.detail1, theme.detail2, 90)

	local detailBg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	detailBg.Name = "RuneDetailBackground"
	detailBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	detailBg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	detailBg.ImageTransparency = 1
	detailBg.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Crop
	detailBg.Parent = details

	local detailText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	detailText.Name = "RuneDetailText"
	detailText.Size = UDim2.new(1, -22, 1, -22)
	detailText.Position = UDim2.new(0, 11, 0, 11)
	detailText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	detailText.TextColor3 = theme.text
	detailText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
	detailText.TextScaled = true
	detailText.TextSize = getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 18 or 22
	detailText.TextWrapped = true
	detailText.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	detailText.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center
	detailText.BorderSizePixel = 0
	detailText.Text = "Выбери руну слева"
	detailText.Parent = details

	local rows = {}
	local function setDetail(runeId)
		if not runeId then return end
		local info = RUNE_EFFECT_INFO[runeId] or RUNE_EFFECT_INFO.Grass or {}
		local stat = rows[runeId] and rows[runeId]:GetAttribute("RuntimeText") or ""
		local asset = getRuneDetailBackgroundAsset(runeId)
		detailBg.Image = asset
		detailBg.ImageTransparency = asset == "" and 1 or 0.42
		detailText.Text = table.concat({
			tostring((runeSystemConfig.names or {})[runeId] or runeId),
			"",
			stat,
			"",
			"За 1 руну: " .. tostring(info.per or "—"),
			"Cap: x" .. formatNumber(info.cap or 1),
		}, "\n")
	end
	for _, runeId in ipairs(runeSystemConfig.displayOrder or {}) do
		local visual = getRuneVisual(runeId)
		local row = Instance.new("TextButton")
		row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 58 or 72)
		row.BackgroundColor3 = theme.row2
		row.BorderSizePixel = 0
		row.Text = ""
		row.Parent = list
		createCorner(row, 12)
		createGradient(row, theme.row1, theme.row2, 0)
		local rowStroke = createStroke(row, theme.accent, 1.4, 0.18)
		pulseStroke(rowStroke, 0.18, 0.38, 1.8)
		local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 34 or 42, 0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 34 or 42)
		icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0.5, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and -17 or -21)
		icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		icon.Image = getRuneIconAsset(runeId)
		icon.Parent = row
		local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		text.Size = UDim2.new(1, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and -48 or -56, 1, -8)
		text.Position = UDim2.new(0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 46 or 54, 0, 4)
		text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		text.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
		text.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Center
		text.TextWrapped = true
		text.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		text.TextSize = getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 12 or 14
		text.TextColor3 = theme.text
		text.Text = tostring((runeSystemConfig.names or {})[runeId] or runeId)
		text.Parent = row
		rows[runeId] = text
		addScaleHover(row)
		row.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			setDetail(runeId)
		end)
	end
	if runeSystemConfig.displayOrder and runeSystemConfig.displayOrder[1] then
		setDetail(runeSystemConfig.displayOrder[1])
	end
	return {rows = rows, details = detailText, detailFrame = details, detailBackground = detailBg}
end

function createRuneStatsBoard(runeSystemConfig)
	if not runeSystemConfig or not runeSystemConfig["id"] then
		warn("Rune stats board skipped: missing rune system config")
		return nil
	end
	if not runeSystemConfig.partStats then return nil end
	local theme = getRuneBoardTheme(runeSystemConfig["id"])
	local _, board = createWorldBoard(runeSystemConfig.statsGuiName, runeSystemConfig.partStats, Enum.NormalId.Front, 72)
	if not board then return nil end
	createHeader(board, runeSystemConfig["id"] .. " RUNE STATS", "Luck / Speed / Bulk / interval")
	local body = Instance.new("Frame")
	body.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, -72)
	body.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 66)
	body.BackgroundColor3 = theme.detail2
	body.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
	body.BorderSizePixel = 0
	body.Parent = board
	createCorner(body, 14)
	createGradient(body, theme.detail1, theme.detail2, 90)
	createStroke(body, theme.accent, 1.3, 0.18)
	local layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
	layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 4 or 6)
	layout.Parent = body
	local padding = Instance.new("UIPadding")
	padding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 6)
	padding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 6)
	padding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 6)
	padding.Parent = body
	return {
		luck = createStatRow(body, "Rune Luck"),
		bulk = createStatRow(body, "Rune Bulk"),
		speed = createStatRow(body, "Rune Speed"),
		total = createStatRow(body, "Итог"),
	}
end

for systemId, cfg in pairs(RUNE_SYSTEM_UI_CONFIG) do
	local indexBoard = createRuneIndexBoard(cfg)
	local statsBoard = createRuneStatsBoard(cfg)
	runeSystemBoards[systemId] = {index = indexBoard, stats = statsBoard}
end

HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER = {"HayAmount", "HayMultiplier", "HayCooldown"}
local hayUpgradeIcons = {}
if type(AssetSlots) == "table" and type(AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons) == "table" then
	hayUpgradeIcons = AssetSlots.UpgradeIcons
end
HAY_UPGRADE_DEFS = {
	HayAmount = {title = "Hay Amount", maxLevel = 250, baseCost = 1, costMultiplier = 3, effectText = "+1 Hay за цикл", bonusText = "+1", fallbackText = "H", icon = tostring(hayUpgradeIcons.HayAmount or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayAmountUpgradeIcon or "")},
	HayMultiplier = {title = "Hay Multiplier", maxLevel = 50, baseCost = 25, costMultiplier = 3, effectText = "+0.5x Hay multiplier", bonusText = "+0.5x", fallbackText = "M", icon = tostring(hayUpgradeIcons.HayMultiplier or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayMultiplierUpgradeIcon or "")},
	HayCooldown = {title = "Hay Cooldown", maxLevel = 25, baseCost = 500, costMultiplier = 2.5, effectText = "-0.1s cooldown", bonusText = "-0.1s", fallbackText = "C", icon = tostring(hayUpgradeIcons.HayCooldown or ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayCooldownUpgradeIcon or "")},
}
hayUpgradeCardsByKey = {}

function getHayUpgradeDefSafe(cardKey)
	local fallbackDefs = {
		HayAmount = {title = "Hay Amount", maxLevel = 250, baseCost = 1, costMultiplier = 3, effectText = "+1 Hay за цикл", bonusText = "+1", fallbackText = "H", icon = tostring(ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayAmountUpgradeIcon or "")},
		HayMultiplier = {title = "Hay Multiplier", maxLevel = 50, baseCost = 25, costMultiplier = 3, effectText = "+0.5x Hay multiplier", bonusText = "+0.5x", fallbackText = "M", icon = tostring(ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayMultiplierUpgradeIcon or "")},
		HayCooldown = {title = "Hay Cooldown", maxLevel = 25, baseCost = 500, costMultiplier = 2.5, effectText = "-0.1s cooldown", bonusText = "-0.1s", fallbackText = "C", icon = tostring(ICON_ASSET_IDS.HayCooldownUpgradeIcon or "")},
	}
	local defs = type(HAY_UPGRADE_DEFS) == "table" and HAY_UPGRADE_DEFS or fallbackDefs
	local def = defs[cardKey]
	if type(def) ~= "table" then
		def = fallbackDefs[cardKey] or {}
	end
	return {
		title = tostring(def.title or cardKey),
		maxLevel = tonumber(def.maxLevel) or 1,
		baseCost = tonumber(def.baseCost) or 1,
		costMultiplier = tonumber(def.costMultiplier) or 1,
		effectText = tostring(def.effectText or ""),
		bonusText = tostring(def.bonusText or ""),
		fallbackText = tostring(def.fallbackText or "H"),
		icon = tostring(def.icon or ""),
	}
end

function getSafeHayUpgrades(data)
	local root = type(data) == "table" and data or {}
	if type(root.HayUpgrades) ~= "table" then
		root.HayUpgrades = {}
	end
	local upgrades = root.HayUpgrades
	local amountValue = tonumber(upgrades.HayAmount)
	local multiplierValue = tonumber(upgrades.HayMultiplier)
	local cooldownValue = tonumber(upgrades.HayCooldown)
	return {
		HayAmount = amountValue or 0,
		HayMultiplier = multiplierValue or 0,
		HayCooldown = cooldownValue or 0,
	}
end

function buildStableHaySnapshot()
	local amountDef = getHayUpgradeDefSafe("HayAmount")
	local multiplierDef = getHayUpgradeDefSafe("HayMultiplier")
	local cooldownDef = getHayUpgradeDefSafe("HayCooldown")
	local safeData = {
		HayCurrency = getValueOrDefault(hayCurrency, 0),
		HayUpgrades = {
			HayAmount = getValueOrDefault(hayAmountLevel, 0),
			HayMultiplier = getValueOrDefault(hayMultiplierLevel, 0),
			HayCooldown = getValueOrDefault(hayCooldownLevel, 0),
		},
		HayCosts = {
			HayAmount = getValueOrDefault(hayAmountCost, amountDef.baseCost),
			HayMultiplier = getValueOrDefault(hayMultiplierCost, multiplierDef.baseCost),
			HayCooldown = getValueOrDefault(hayCooldownCost, cooldownDef.baseCost),
		},
	}
	local safeUpgrades = getSafeHayUpgrades(safeData)
	return {
		HayCurrency = tonumber(safeData.HayCurrency) or 0,
		HayUpgrades = safeUpgrades,
		HayCosts = {
			HayAmount = tonumber(safeData.HayCosts.HayAmount) or amountDef.baseCost,
			HayMultiplier = tonumber(safeData.HayCosts.HayMultiplier) or multiplierDef.baseCost,
			HayCooldown = tonumber(safeData.HayCosts.HayCooldown) or cooldownDef.baseCost,
		},
	}
end

function getHayUpgradeCard(cardKey)
	if type(hayUpgradeCardsByKey) ~= "table" then
		hayUpgradeCardsByKey = {}
	end
	return hayUpgradeCardsByKey[cardKey]
end

function readHayUpgradeLevel(snapshot, cardKey)
	local root = type(snapshot) == "table" and snapshot or {}
	local upgrades = getSafeHayUpgrades(root)
	return tonumber(upgrades[cardKey]) or 0
end

function readHayUpgradeCost(snapshot, cardKey)
	local root = type(snapshot) == "table" and snapshot or {}
	local costs = type(root.HayCosts) == "table" and root.HayCosts or {}
	local def = getHayUpgradeDefSafe(cardKey)
	return tonumber(costs[cardKey]) or def.baseCost
end
if hayUpgradeBoardPart then
	local _, hayUpgradeBoard = createWorldBoard("HayUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", hayUpgradeBoardPart, Enum.NormalId.Front, 72)
	createHeader(hayUpgradeBoard, "HAY UPGRADES", "Amount / Multiplier / Cooldown")
	local hayScroll = createHorizontalScroller(hayUpgradeBoard, 66, 12)
	local hayCardPaletteByKey = {
		HayAmount = {system = "Hay", card1 = Color3.fromRGB(121, 215, 158), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(73, 175, 120), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(176, 241, 200), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(105, 202, 148), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 238, 159), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(232, 186, 79)},
		HayMultiplier = {system = "Hay", card1 = Color3.fromRGB(98, 161, 236), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(71, 123, 196), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(160, 205, 255), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(113, 166, 234), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(214, 230, 255), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(145, 173, 245)},
		HayCooldown = {system = "Hay", card1 = Color3.fromRGB(182, 140, 236), card2 = Color3.fromRGB(146, 97, 213), inner1 = Color3.fromRGB(224, 192, 255), inner2 = Color3.fromRGB(177, 129, 236), icon1 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 222, 244), icon2 = Color3.fromRGB(232, 174, 255)},
	}
	for idx = 1, #HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER do
		local key = HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER[idx]
		local def = getHayUpgradeDefSafe(key)
		hayUpgradeCardsByKey[key] = createUpgradeCard(
			hayScroll,
			def.title,
			def.effectText,
			def.bonusText,
			def.icon,
			def.fallbackText,
			hayCardPaletteByKey[key]
		)
	end
end

function getValueOrDefault(valueObject, defaultValue)
	if valueObject and valueObject.Value ~= nil then
		local numeric = tonumber(valueObject.Value)
		if numeric ~= nil then
			return numeric
		end
	end
	return defaultValue
end

function getRarityColor(rarity)
	if rarity == "Secret" then return Color3.fromRGB(255, 66, 66) end
	if rarity == "Mythic" then return Color3.fromRGB(255, 112, 184) end
	if rarity == "Legendary" then return Color3.fromRGB(255, 197, 92) end
	if rarity == "Epic" then return Color3.fromRGB(204, 133, 255) end
	if rarity == "Rare" then return Color3.fromRGB(97, 171, 255) end
	if rarity == "Uncommon" then return Color3.fromRGB(124, 210, 139) end
	return Color3.fromRGB(198, 212, 238)
end

function getPassiveStyle(passiveId, rarity)
	if rarity == "Secret" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(26, 8, 8), Color3.fromRGB(255, 72, 72), Color3.fromRGB(8, 8, 8)
	elseif rarity == "Mythic" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(68, 16, 24), Color3.fromRGB(255, 88, 88), Color3.fromRGB(255, 124, 124)
	elseif rarity == "Legendary" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(84, 62, 18), Color3.fromRGB(255, 205, 95), Color3.fromRGB(255, 238, 172)
	elseif rarity == "Epic" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(54, 28, 78), Color3.fromRGB(182, 115, 255), Color3.fromRGB(230, 188, 255)
	elseif rarity == "Rare" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(25, 50, 86), Color3.fromRGB(112, 186, 255), Color3.fromRGB(172, 231, 255)
	elseif rarity == "Common" then
		return Color3.fromRGB(34, 36, 42), Color3.fromRGB(114, 120, 134), Color3.fromRGB(176, 184, 204)
	end
	local seed = 0
	for i = 1, #tostring(passiveId or "") do
		seed += string.byte(passiveId, i)
	end
	local base = getRarityColor(rarity)
	local tint = Color3.fromRGB(70 + (seed % 80), 90 + (seed * 3 % 80), 120 + (seed * 5 % 80))
	return base:Lerp(tint, 0.45), base, tint
end

function decorateCardCorners(parent)
	local top = Instance.new("Frame")
	top.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 2)
	top.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 4)
	top.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	top.BorderSizePixel = 0
	top.Parent = parent
	local bottom = top:Clone()
	bottom.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 1, -6)
	bottom.Parent = parent
	local left = Instance.new("Frame")
	left.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 1, -8)
	left.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 4)
	left.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	left.BorderSizePixel = 0
	left.Parent = parent
	local right = left:Clone()
	right.Position = UDim2.new(1, -6, 0, 4)
	right.Parent = parent
end

function getCurrencyColor(currencyType)
	if currencyType == "Wood" then return Color3.fromRGB(121, 194, 118) end
	if currencyType == "Paper" then return Color3.fromRGB(214, 221, 255) end
	return Color3.fromRGB(252, 206, 104)
end

function createPassiveUi()
	local ui = {
		indexPanel = nil,
		inventoryPanel = nil,
		hintGui = nil,
		hintEmoji = nil,
		rollButton = nil,
		rollButtonInventory = nil,
		slots = {},
		indexButtons = {},
		indexDetail = nil,
		rollFxLayer = nil,
		equippedText = nil,
		lastState = {inventory = {}, equippedUid = ""},
	}

	if not passiveInventoryBlock then
		return ui
	end

	ui.hintGui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
	ui.hintGui.Name = "PassiveHintGui"
	ui.hintGui.Adornee = passiveInventoryBlock
	ui.hintGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 260, 0, 140)
	ui.hintGui.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 4.5, 0)
	ui.hintGui.AlwaysOnTop = true
	ui.hintGui.MaxDistance = 28
	ui.hintGui.Parent = screenGui

	local circle = Instance.new("Frame")
	circle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 120, 0, 120)
	circle.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -60, 0.45, -60)
	circle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(104, 150, 237)
	circle.BorderSizePixel = 0
	circle.Parent = ui.hintGui
	createCorner(circle, 999)
	createGradient(circle, Color3.fromRGB(160, 199, 255), Color3.fromRGB(94, 126, 214), 90)
	createStroke(circle, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), 2, 0.15)

	local arrow = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	arrow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	arrow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28)
	arrow.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -22)
	arrow.Text = "▼ ПАССИВЫ ТУТ ▼"
	arrow.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(246, 250, 255)
	arrow.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack

	arrow.Parent = circle

	ui.hintEmoji = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	ui.hintEmoji.BackgroundTransparency = 1

	ui.hintEmoji.TextScaled = false
	ui.hintEmoji.TextSize = 64
	ui.hintEmoji.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	ui.hintEmoji.Parent = circle

	ui.rollFxLayer = Instance.new("Frame")
	ui.rollFxLayer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	ui.rollFxLayer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	ui.rollFxLayer.Visible = false
	ui.rollFxLayer.ZIndex = 90
	ui.rollFxLayer.Parent = screenGui

	ui.indexPanel = Instance.new("Frame")
	ui.indexPanel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 700, 0, 500)
	ui.indexPanel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	ui.indexPanel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.55, 0)
	ui.indexPanel.Visible = false
	ui.indexPanel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(12, 22, 14)
	ui.indexPanel.BorderSizePixel = 0
	ui.indexPanel.Parent = screenGui
	ui.indexPanel:SetAttribute("CompactWidePanel", true)
	applyResponsivePanel(ui.indexPanel, 0.74, 0.76, 980, 620, UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.55, 0))
	createCorner(ui.indexPanel, 20)
	createGradient(ui.indexPanel, Color3.fromRGB(40, 66, 44), Color3.fromRGB(14, 24, 16), 90)
	createStroke(ui.indexPanel, Color3.fromRGB(152, 255, 102), 2, 0.08)

	createHeader(ui.indexPanel, "PASSIVE INDEX", "Нажми на пассив и смотри статы")
	local closeIndexBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
	closeIndexBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
	closeIndexBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 8)

	closeIndexBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

	closeIndexBtn.TextScaled = true

	ui.rollButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack

	createGradient(ui.rollButton, Color3.fromRGB(255, 226, 126), Color3.fromRGB(183, 107, 255), 0)
	createStroke(ui.rollButton, Color3.fromRGB(255, 242, 180), 1.4, 0.1)
	addScaleHover(ui.rollButton)

	local openInvButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
	openInvButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
	openInvButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 70)
	openInvButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(166, 196, 106)
	openInvButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 46, 23)
	openInvButton.Text = "ОТКРЫТЬ ИНВЕНТАРЬ"
	openInvButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	openInvButton.TextScaled = true
	openInvButton.Parent = ui.indexPanel
	createCorner(openInvButton, 12)
	createGradient(openInvButton, Color3.fromRGB(202, 174, 255), Color3.fromRGB(94, 125, 255), 0)
	createStroke(openInvButton, Color3.fromRGB(230, 214, 255), 1.4, 0.14)
	addScaleHover(openInvButton)

	local indexList = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
	indexList.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 1, -122)
	indexList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
	indexList.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	indexList.BorderSizePixel = 0
	indexList.ScrollBarThickness = getGuiPreset().scrollBar
	indexList.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(202, 174, 255)
	indexList.ElasticBehavior = Enum.ElasticBehavior.WhenScrollable
	indexList.ScrollingDirection = Enum.ScrollingDirection.Y
	indexList.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	indexList.Parent = ui.indexPanel
	applyFreeScroll(indexList, {minCanvasY = 480})
	local grid = Instance.new("UIGridLayout")
	grid.CellSize = UDim2.new(0, 122, 0, 116)
	grid.CellPadding = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 12)
	grid.Parent = indexList
	local function refreshIndexGrid()
		local view = workspace.CurrentCamera and workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize or Vector2.new(1280,720)
		local profile = getDeviceProfile()
		local columns = profile == "mobile" and 2 or (profile == "tablet" and 3 or 5)
		local pad = profile == "mobile" and 14 or 10
		grid.CellPadding = UDim2.new(0, pad, 0, pad + 2)
		local width = math.floor((indexList.AbsoluteSize.X - (columns - 1) * pad - 12) / columns)
		width = math.max(profile == "mobile" and 132 or 108, width)
		grid.CellSize = UDim2.new(0, width, 0, profile == "mobile" and 118 or 122)
	end
	grid:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
		indexList.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, grid.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 12)
	end)
	indexList:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteSize"):Connect(refreshIndexGrid)
	if workspace.CurrentCamera then
		workspace.CurrentCamera:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ViewportSize"):Connect(refreshIndexGrid)
	end
	refreshIndexGrid()

	for passiveId, passiveDef in pairs(PASSIVE_DEFS) do
		local b = Instance.new("TextButton")
		b.Text = ""
		b.Size = UDim2.new(0, 122, 0, 116)
		b.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 18, 24)
		b.BackgroundTransparency = 0.12
		b.BorderSizePixel = 0
		b.Parent = indexList
		createCorner(b, 12)
		local g1, g2, g3 = getPassiveStyle(passiveId, passiveDef.rarity)
		b.BackgroundColor3 = g1
		-- no default tint fill; card uses explicit image background when provided
		local outline = createStroke(b, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), 2.2, 0.02)
		pulseStroke(outline, 0.02, passiveDef.rarity == "Common" and 0.18 or 0.32, passiveDef.rarity == "Mythic" and 0.9 or 1.7)
		decorateCardCorners(b)
		createStroke(b, g2, 1.2, 0.2)
		createGradient(b, g1, g3, 35)
		local customBg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		customBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		customBg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		customBg.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.PassiveIndexBackgrounds[passiveId])
		customBg.ImageTransparency = customBg.Image == "" and 1 or 0
		customBg.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Crop
		customBg.Parent = b
		if passiveDef.rarity == "Mythic" or passiveDef.rarity == "Secret" then
			local rainbow = Instance.new("UIGradient")
			rainbow.Color = ColorSequence.new({
				ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 95, 172)),
				ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.33, Color3.fromRGB(101, 196, 255)),
				ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.66, Color3.fromRGB(158, 255, 126)),
				ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 212, 108)),
			})
			rainbow.Parent = outline
		end
		local cardIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		cardIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)
		cardIcon.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
		cardIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 8)
		cardIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		cardIcon.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.IndexCardImages[passiveId] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.PassiveCardDefault)
		cardIcon.Parent = b
		local shine = Instance.new("Frame")
		shine.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 18)
		shine.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 4)
		shine.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		shine.BackgroundTransparency = 0.9
		shine.BorderSizePixel = 0
		shine.Parent = b
		createCorner(shine, 8)
		local deco = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		deco.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
		deco.Position = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 4)
		deco.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		deco.Text = passiveDef.rarity == "Mythic" and "✦" or "✧"
		deco.TextColor3 = getRarityColor(passiveDef.rarity)
		deco.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
		deco.TextScaled = true
		deco.Parent = b
		local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")

	local function refreshPassivePanelsForDevice()
		local profile = getDeviceProfile()
		if profile == "mobile" then
			closeIndexBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			closeInvBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			closeInvBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 8)

			backToIndex.Position = UDim2.new(1, -144, 0, 8)

			ui.rollButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 68)
			openInvButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 112, 0, 34)
			openInvButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 8)
			indexList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 110)
			indexList.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 1, -118)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Size = UDim2.new(0.58, -12, 0, 34)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 70)
			ui.equippedText.Size = UDim2.new(0.42, -12, 0, 34)
			ui.equippedText.Position = UDim2.new(0.58, 4, 0, 70)
			ui.slotsList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
			ui.slotsList.Size = UDim2.new(0.58, -12, 1, -122)
			ui.managePanel.Position = UDim2.new(0.58, 4, 0, 114)
			ui.managePanel.Size = UDim2.new(0.42, -12, 1, -122)
			ui.manageInfo.Size = UDim2.new(1, -14, 1, -118)
			ui.manageInfo.TextScaled = false
			ui.manageInfo.TextSize = 13
			ui.equipBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.82, 0, 0, 30)
			ui.equipBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.09, 0, 1, -70)
			ui.equipBtn.TextSize = 14
			ui.deleteBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.82, 0, 0, 30)
			ui.deleteBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.09, 0, 1, -34)
			ui.deleteBtn.TextSize = 14
		elseif profile == "tablet" then
			closeIndexBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			ui.rollButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.rollButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 70)
			openInvButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			openInvButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 70)
			indexList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
			indexList.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 1, -122)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 70)
			ui.equippedText.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.equippedText.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 70)
			ui.slotsList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
			closeInvBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			closeInvBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 8)
			backToIndex.Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 34)
			backToIndex.Position = UDim2.new(1, -188, 0, 8)
			ui.slotsList.Size = UDim2.new(0.48, -8, 1, -122)
			ui.managePanel.Position = UDim2.new(0.48, 8, 0, 114)
			ui.managePanel.Size = UDim2.new(0.52, -8, 1, -122)
			ui.manageInfo.Size = UDim2.new(1, -14, 1, -128)
			ui.manageInfo.TextScaled = false
			ui.manageInfo.TextSize = 14
			ui.equipBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.82, 0, 0, 34)
			ui.equipBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.09, 0, 1, -80)
			ui.equipBtn.TextSize = 14
			ui.deleteBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.82, 0, 0, 34)
			ui.deleteBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.09, 0, 1, -40)
			ui.deleteBtn.TextSize = 14
		else
			closeIndexBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			ui.rollButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.rollButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 70)
			openInvButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			openInvButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 70)
			indexList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
			indexList.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 1, -122)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.rollButtonInventory.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 70)
			ui.equippedText.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -12, 0, 40)
			ui.equippedText.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 70)
			ui.slotsList.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 114)
			closeInvBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
			closeInvBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 8)
			backToIndex.Size = UDim2.new(0, 140, 0, 34)
			backToIndex.Position = UDim2.new(1, -188, 0, 8)
			ui.slotsList.Size = UDim2.new(0.48, -8, 1, -122)
			ui.managePanel.Position = UDim2.new(0.48, 8, 0, 114)
			ui.managePanel.Size = UDim2.new(0.52, -8, 1, -122)
			ui.manageInfo.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 1, -168)
			ui.manageInfo.TextScaled = false
			ui.manageInfo.TextSize = 16
			ui.equipBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 36)
			ui.equipBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 1, -118)
			ui.deleteBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 36)
			ui.deleteBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 1, -76)
		end
	end
	refreshPassivePanelsForDevice()
	if workspace.CurrentCamera then
		workspace.CurrentCamera:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ViewportSize"):Connect(refreshPassivePanelsForDevice)
	end

	openInvButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.indexPanel, false)
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.inventoryPanel, true)
	end)
	closeIndexBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.indexPanel, false)
	end)
	closeInvBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.inventoryPanel, false)
	end)
	backToIndex.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.inventoryPanel, false)
		animatePanelVisibility(ui.indexPanel, true)
	end)
	closeDetail.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		ui.indexDetail.Visible = false
	end)
	if ui.deleteConfirmNo then
		ui.deleteConfirmNo.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			ui.deleteConfirm.Visible = false
		end)
	end
	for button, passiveId in pairs(ui.indexButtons) do
		button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			local def = PASSIVE_DEFS[passiveId]
			if not def then
				return
			end
			local bonusLines = getPassiveBonusLines(def)
			detailText.Text = table.concat({
				def.name .. " [" .. tostring(def.rarity) .. "]",
				"Шанс: " .. tostring(def.chance or "?"),
				"",
				"Бонусы:",
				table.concat(bonusLines, "\n"),
			}, "\n")
			ui.indexDetail.Visible = true
		end)
	end

	return ui
end

passiveUi = createPassiveUi()

function openPassiveIndexCard(passiveId)
	if not passiveUi or not passiveUi.indexDetail then
		return
	end
	local def = PASSIVE_DEFS[passiveId]
	if not def then
		return
	end
	local icon = passiveUi.indexDetail:FindFirstChild("CardIcon")
	if not icon then
		icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		icon.Name = "CardIcon"
		icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 84, 0, 84)
		icon.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
		icon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 10)
		icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		icon.Parent = passiveUi.indexDetail
	end
	icon.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.PassiveCardImages[passiveId] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.PassiveCardDefault)
	local detailText = passiveUi.indexDetail:FindFirstChild("Text")
	if detailText and detailText:IsA("TextLabel") then
		local bonusLines = getPassiveBonusLines(def)
		detailText.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 100)
		detailText.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, -148)
		detailText.Text = table.concat({
			def.name .. " [" .. tostring(def.rarity) .. "]",
			"Шанс: " .. tostring(def.chance or "?"),
			"",
			"Бонусы:",
			table.concat(bonusLines, "\n"),
		}, "\n")
	end
	passiveUi.indexDetail.Visible = true
end

for button, passiveId in pairs(passiveUi.indexButtons or {}) do
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		openPassiveIndexCard(passiveId)
	end)
end

function createRuneOverlays()
	runeUi.summaryRows = {}
	runeUi.chanceRows = {}
	runeUi.sessionRows = {}

	function createRuneBillboard(adornee, name, size, offset, backgroundSlot)
		local gui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
		gui.Name = name
		gui.Adornee = adornee
		gui.Size = size
		gui.StudsOffset = offset
		gui.AlwaysOnTop = true
		gui.MaxDistance = 20
		gui.LightInfluence = 0
		gui.Parent = screenGui

		local root = Instance.new("Frame")
		root.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		root.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(27, 94, 21)
		root.BorderSizePixel = 0
		root.Parent = gui

		createGradient(root, Color3.fromRGB(77, 156, 33), Color3.fromRGB(19, 72, 18), 90)

		local bgImage = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		bgImage.Name = "TemplateBackground"
		bgImage.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		bgImage.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		bgImage.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.BillboardBackgrounds[backgroundSlot])
		bgImage.ImageTransparency = bgImage.Image == "" and 1 or 0
		bgImage.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Stretch
		bgImage.Parent = root

		local header = Instance.new("Frame")
		header.Size = UDim2.new(1, -18, 0, 44)
		header.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 6)
		header.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 110, 34)
		header.BorderSizePixel = 0
		header.Parent = root
		createCorner(header, 14)
		createStroke(header, Color3.fromRGB(26, 66, 24), 3, 0)
		createGradient(header, Color3.fromRGB(74, 141, 52), Color3.fromRGB(23, 80, 26), 90)

		local headerText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		headerText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		headerText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		headerText.Text = "◈  РУНЫ  ◈"
		headerText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 248, 255)
		headerText.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.45

			rowHolder.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, rowList.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 6)

			iconBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 18, 26)
			iconBadge.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
			iconBadge.BorderSizePixel = 0

	end

	function createRuneSessionScreen()
		local panel = Instance.new("Frame")
		panel.Name = "RuneSessionPanel"
		panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 210, 0, 262)
		panel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 1)
		panel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -14, 1, -14)
		if getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" then
			panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 168, 0, 214)
			panel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -8, 1, -8)
		elseif getDeviceProfile() == "tablet" then
			panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 188, 0, 236)
		end
		local desktopRuneUi = getDeviceProfile() ~= "mobile" and getDeviceProfile() ~= "tablet"
		if desktopRuneUi then
			panel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 340)
		end
		panel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 80, 20)
		panel.BorderSizePixel = 0
		panel.Visible = false
		panel.Parent = screenGui
		createCorner(panel, 14)
		local sessionStroke = createStroke(panel, Color3.fromRGB(148, 255, 83), 3, 0.02)
		pulseStroke(sessionStroke, 0.02, 0.32, 1.15)
		createGradient(panel, Color3.fromRGB(35, 90, 34), Color3.fromRGB(7, 18, 17), 90)

		local bgImage = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		bgImage.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		bgImage.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		bgImage.Image = ""
		bgImage.ImageTransparency = 1
		bgImage.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Stretch
		bgImage.Parent = panel

		local header = Instance.new("Frame")
		header.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 30)
		header.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 6)
		header.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 110, 34)
		header.BorderSizePixel = 0
		header.Parent = panel
		createCorner(header, 12)
		createStroke(header, Color3.fromRGB(26, 66, 24), 2, 0)
		local headerText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		headerText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		headerText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		headerText.Text = desktopRuneUi and "◈  RUNE SESSION  ◈" or "◈  РУНЫ  ◈"
		headerText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 248, 255)
		headerText.TextStrokeTransparency = desktopRuneUi and 0.15 or 0.35
		headerText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
		headerText.TextScaled = true
		headerText.Parent = header

		local listHolder = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
		listHolder.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 1, -42)
		listHolder.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 36)
		listHolder.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		listHolder.BorderSizePixel = 0
		listHolder.ScrollBarThickness = getGuiPreset().scrollBar
		if desktopRuneUi then
			listHolder.ScrollBarThickness = math.max(18, getGuiPreset().scrollBar + 6)
			listHolder.ScrollingDirection = Enum.ScrollingDirection.XY
		else
			listHolder.ScrollingDirection = Enum.ScrollingDirection.Y
		end
		listHolder.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(196, 255, 124)
		listHolder.ScrollBarImageTransparency = 1
		listHolder.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
		listHolder.Parent = panel
		applyFreeScroll(listHolder, {minCanvasX = 260, minCanvasY = 420})

		local list = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
		list.Padding = UDim.new(0, 5)
		list.Parent = listHolder
		list.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
		list.VerticalAlignment = Enum.VerticalAlignment.Top
		list:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
			local xPad = desktopRuneUi and 220 or 0
			listHolder.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, xPad, 0, list.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + (desktopRuneUi and 90 or 4))
		end)

		for _, runeId in ipairs({"Grass", "DarkGrass", "Dandelion", "Flower", "Violet", "Rose", "Palka", "ObrublennyKonec", "VetvDereva", "Brevno", "Poleno", "ObgorevshiyPen"}) do
			local visual = getRuneVisual(runeId)
			local row = Instance.new("Frame")
			row.Name = runeId .. "SessionRow"
			row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, getDeviceProfile() == "mobile" and 30 or 34)
			row.BackgroundColor3 = visual.rowColor
			row.BorderSizePixel = 0
			row.Parent = listHolder
			createCorner(row, 12)
			createGradient(row, visual.rowColor, Color3.fromRGB(10, 18, 20), 0)
			local runeRowStroke = createStroke(row, visual.accent, 2, 0.08)
			pulseStroke(runeRowStroke, 0.08, 0.34, 1.4)

			-- Rune icon
			local iconFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
			iconFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 24, 0, 24)
			iconFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0.5, -12)
			iconFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(12, 16, 24)
			iconFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
			iconFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
			iconFrame.Parent = row
			createCorner(iconFrame, 999)
			createStroke(iconFrame, visual.accent, 2, 0)

			local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
			icon.Size = UDim2.new(1, -6, 1, -6)
			icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 3)
			icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
			icon.Image = getRuneIconAsset(runeId)
			icon.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
			icon.Parent = iconFrame

			-- Name label
			local nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
			nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -82, 1, 0)
			nameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 0)
			nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
			nameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
			nameLabel.Text = ((RUNE_SYSTEM_UI_CONFIG.Nature.names or {})[runeId]) or ((RUNE_SYSTEM_UI_CONFIG.Forest.names or {})[runeId]) or visual.name
			nameLabel.TextColor3 = visual.accent
			nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
			nameLabel.TextScaled = true
			nameLabel.Parent = row

			-- Gain label: "+1-99" style, right side
			local gain = Instance.new("TextLabel")
			gain.Name = "Gain"
			gain.Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 1, 0)
			gain.Position = UDim2.new(1, -46, 0, 0)
			gain.BackgroundTransparency = 1
			gain.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
			gain.Text = "+0"
			gain.TextColor3 = visual.accent
			gain.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
			gain.TextScaled = true
			gain.Parent = row
			runeUi.sessionRows[runeId] = gain
			row.Visible = false
		end

		runeUi.sessionPanel = panel
	end

	createRuneSessionScreen()
end

forestRuneSessionCounts = {Palka = 0, ObrublennyKonec = 0, VetvDereva = 0, Brevno = 0, Poleno = 0, ObgorevshiyPen = 0}

	for _, runeId in ipairs({"Palka", "ObrublennyKonec", "VetvDereva", "Brevno", "Poleno", "ObgorevshiyPen"}) do

		row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2

		createCorner(row, 8)

		iconWrap.Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 26)
		iconWrap.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0.5, -13)
		iconWrap.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 26, 17)
		iconWrap.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
		iconWrap.BorderSizePixel = 0
		iconWrap.Parent = row
		createCorner(iconWrap, 999)
		createStroke(iconWrap, Color3.fromRGB(160, 128, 82), 1.2, 0.2)
