function getRuneSessionOrder(systemName)
	local cfg = RUNE_SYSTEM_UI_CONFIG[systemName or activeRuneSystem or "Nature"]
	return (cfg and cfg.displayOrder) or RUNE_DISPLAY_ORDER
end

function updateRuneSession(systemName, session)
	activeRuneSystem = systemName or activeRuneSystem or "Nature"
	local order = getRuneSessionOrder(activeRuneSystem)
	runeSessionCounts = {}
	for _, runeId in ipairs(order) do
		runeSessionCounts[runeId] = tonumber(session and session[runeId]) or tonumber(runeSessionCounts[runeId]) or 0
	end
	if runeUi.sessionRows then
		for runeId, label in pairs(runeUi.sessionRows) do
			local visible = runeSessionCounts[runeId] ~= nil
			label.Visible = visible
			if label.Parent then label.Parent.Visible = visible end
			label.Text = "+" .. formatNumber(runeSessionCounts[runeId] or 0)
		end
	end
end

function updateRuneSessionGui()
	updateRuneSession(activeRuneSystem, runeSessionCounts)
end

function updateRuneSummaryGui()
	local state = parseRuneState()
	local counts = state.counts or {}
	for _, runeId in ipairs(RUNE_DISPLAY_ORDER) do
		local label = runeUi.summaryRows and runeUi.summaryRows[runeId]
		local chanceLabel = runeUi.chanceRows and runeUi.chanceRows[runeId]
		if label then
			local count = tonumber(counts[runeId]) or 0
			label.Text = formatNumber(count)
		end
		if chanceLabel then
			local baseDenom = tonumber(effectiveRuneDenominators[runeId]) or tonumber(RUNE_VISUALS[runeId] and RUNE_VISUALS[runeId].baseDenominator) or 1
			local finalLuck = select(1, getFinalRuneStats())
			local denom = math.max(1, math.floor((baseDenom / math.max(1, finalLuck)) + 0.5))
			chanceLabel.Text = "1 / " .. tostring(denom)
		end
	end
end

function updateRuneWorldDisplay()
	refreshRuneStats()
	updateRuneSessionGui()
end

function refreshRuneStats()
	local ok = pcall(function()
		updateRuneSummaryGui()
		updateRuneSessionGui()
		for _, bundle in pairs(runeSystemBoards or {}) do
			if bundle and bundle.stats and bundle.stats.luck then
				local effLuck, effSpeed, effBulk = getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
				local speedOverflowBulk = getRuneSpeedOverflowBulk(effSpeed)
				local effBulkBonus = math.max(0, effBulk - 1)
				local speedSeconds = getRuneRollIntervalFromSpeed(effSpeed)
				bundle.stats.luck.Text = formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x"
				bundle.stats.bulk.Text = "+" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
				bundle.stats.speed.Text = string.format("%ss/roll | Overflow Bulk +%s", formatRuneStatValue(speedSeconds), formatRuneStatValue(speedOverflowBulk))
				bundle.stats.total.Text = "Luck " .. formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x | Speed " .. formatRuneStatValue(effSpeed) .. "x | Bulk +" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
			end
		end
	end)
	return ok
end

function startRuneRolling(systemName)
	runeRollingActive = true
	activeRuneSystem = systemName or activeRuneSystem or "Nature"
	updateRuneSession(activeRuneSystem, {})
	if runeUi.sessionPanel then
		runeUi.sessionPanel.Visible = true
	end
	updateRuneSessionGui()
	refreshRuneStats()
end

function stopRuneRolling(systemName)
	if systemName and activeRuneSystem and systemName ~= activeRuneSystem then
		return
	end
	runeRollingActive = false
	if runeUi.sessionPanel then
		runeUi.sessionPanel.Visible = false
	end
end

function parsePassiveState()
	local ok, decoded = pcall(function()
		return HttpService:JSONDecode(passiveStateJson.Value)
	end)
	if ok and type(decoded) == "table" and type(decoded.inventory) == "table" then
		return decoded
	end
	return {inventory = {}, equippedUid = ""}
end

parseRuneState = function()
	local ok, decoded = pcall(function()
		return HttpService:JSONDecode(runeStateJson.Value)
	end)
	if ok and type(decoded) == "table" then
		if type(decoded.natureCounts) == "table" then
			decoded.counts = decoded.natureCounts
		end
		if type(decoded.counts) == "table" then
			return decoded
		end
	end
	return {counts = {Grass = 0, DarkGrass = 0, Dandelion = 0, Flower = 0, Violet = 0, Rose = 0}}
end

function getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local state = parsePassiveState()
	local passiveInventory = (state and state.inventory) or {}
	for _, entry in ipairs(passiveInventory) do
		if type(entry) == "table" and entry.uid and entry.passiveId and entry.uid == state.equippedUid then
			return PASSIVE_DEFS[entry.passiveId]
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function getCoinUpgradeMultiplier()
	return 1 + (coinMultiplierLevel.Value * 0.1)
end

function getCoinReward()
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveCoin = passive and (passive.coinMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveGlobal = passive and (passive.globalMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local baseValue = 1 + coinValueLevel.Value
	local woodCoinBoostMultiplier = 1.1 ^ woodCoinBoostLevel.Value
	local coinGoalBoostMultiplier = fourthSystemsUnlocked.Value and select(1, computeGoalWoodFactor(coins.Value)) or 1
	return roundToTenth(baseValue * getCoinUpgradeMultiplier() * rebirthCoinMultiplierBonus.Value * coinGoalBoostMultiplier * woodCoinBoostMultiplier * passiveCoin * passiveGlobal)
end

function getCoinRespawn()
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveSpeed = passive and (passive.speedMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local value = 3 - (coinSpawnLevel.Value * 0.5) - rebirthSpawnSpeedBonus.Value
	value /= math.max(1, passiveSpeed)
	if value < 0.5 then
		value = 0.5
	end
	return roundToTenth(value)
end

function computeGoalWoodFactor(coinAmount)
	local threshold = 10000
	local goalsReached = 0
	local factor = 1

	while factor < 10 and coinAmount >= threshold do
		goalsReached += 1
		factor = math.min(1 + (goalsReached * 0.1), 10)
		threshold = math.floor(threshold * 1.25 + 0.5)
	end

	return factor, goalsReached, threshold
end

function getWoodReward()
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveWood = passive and (passive.woodMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveGlobal = passive and (passive.globalMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local baseValue = 1 + woodValueLevel.Value
	local baseMultiplier = 1 + woodMultiplierLevel.Value + (coinWoodBoostLevel.Value * 0.25)

	local goalFactor = 1
	if fourthSystemsUnlocked.Value then
		goalFactor = select(1, computeGoalWoodFactor(coins.Value))
	end

	return roundToTenth(baseValue * baseMultiplier * goalFactor * rebirthWoodMultiplierBonus.Value * passiveWood * passiveGlobal)
end

function getWoodCooldown()
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveSpeed = passive and (passive.speedMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local value = 3 - (woodSpeedLevel.Value * 0.25)
	if value < 0.5 then
		value = 0.5
	end
	return roundToTenth(value / math.max(1, passiveSpeed))
end

function getClientXpPerCollectEstimate()
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveXpMul = passive and (passive.xpMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local baseXpPerCoin = 1 + (tonumber(xpMultiplierLevel and xpMultiplierLevel.Value) or 0)
	local boostMul = 1 + (tonumber(xpBoostLevel and xpBoostLevel.Value) or 0)
	local eventMul = isAdminEventActive("StatsX2") and 2 or 1
	return roundToTenth(baseXpPerCoin * boostMul * passiveXpMul * eventMul)
end

function isAdminEventActive(eventKey)
	for _, ev in ipairs(activeAdminEvents or {}) do
		local eventData = type(ev) == "table" and ev or {}
		if eventData.key == eventKey and (tonumber(eventData.timeLeft) or 0) > 0 then
			return true
		end
	end
	return false
end

getActiveAdminEventUpgrades = function() return 1, 1, 1, 0 end

function getRuneSpeedOverflowBulk(speedStat)
	local interval = 1 / math.max(1, (1 + (math.max(0, speedStat) * 0.5)))
	if interval >= 0.01 then
		return 0
	end
	local overflowFactor = math.min(250, 0.01 / math.max(0.000001, interval))
	return math.max(0, math.floor((overflowFactor - 1) * 2 + 0.5))
end

function getRuneRollIntervalFromSpeed(speedStat)
	local baseInterval = 1 / math.max(1, (1 + (math.max(0, speedStat) * 0.5)))
	return math.max(0.01, baseInterval)
end

function formatRuneStatValue(value)
	local v = tonumber(value) or 0
	local rounded = math.floor(v * 10 + 0.5) / 10
	if math.abs(rounded - math.floor(rounded + 0.0001)) < 0.0001 then
		return tostring(math.floor(rounded + 0.0001))
	end
	return string.format("%.1f", rounded)
end

function getFinalRuneStats()
	local baseLuck = 1 + runeLuckLevel.Value + runeLuckXpLevel.Value
	local baseSpeed = 1 + runeSpeedLevel.Value + runeSpeedXpLevel.Value
	local baseBulkBonus = runeBulkLevel.Value + runeBulkXpLevel.Value
	local runeState = parseRuneState()
	local runeCounts = runeState.counts or {}
	local mythicCount = tonumber(runeCounts.Mythic) or 0
	local mythicLuckSpeedMul = math.min(5, 1 + (mythicCount * 0.1))
	local mythicBulkAdd = math.min(25, math.floor(mythicCount * 0.5 + 0.5))
	local passive = getEquippedPassiveDef()
	local passiveLuckMul = passive and (passive.runeLuckMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveSpeedMul = passive and (passive.runeSpeedMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveBulkMul = passive and (passive.runeBulkMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveGlobalMul = passive and (passive.globalMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local passiveCommonSpeedMul = passive and (passive.speedMultiplier or 1) or 1
	local eventLuckMul, eventSpeedMul, eventBulkMul, eventBulkAdd = getActiveAdminEventUpgrades()
	local gamepassLuckMul = tripleRuneLuckGamepass and tripleRuneLuckGamepass.Value and 3 or 1
	local rawLuck = baseLuck * passiveLuckMul * passiveGlobalMul * mythicLuckSpeedMul * eventLuckMul * gamepassLuckMul
	local luckSoftCapKnee = 25
	local luck = rawLuck <= luckSoftCapKnee and rawLuck or (luckSoftCapKnee + math.sqrt(math.max(0, rawLuck - luckSoftCapKnee)) * 3.5)
	local speed = baseSpeed * passiveSpeedMul * passiveGlobalMul * passiveCommonSpeedMul * mythicLuckSpeedMul * eventSpeedMul
	local bulkBonus = (baseBulkBonus + mythicBulkAdd) * passiveBulkMul * passiveGlobalMul
	bulkBonus = bulkBonus * eventBulkMul + eventBulkAdd
	if rebirthCount.Value >= 7 then
		luck = luck * 1.5
	end
	bulkBonus += getRuneSpeedOverflowBulk(speed)
	local bulk = math.max(1, 1 + math.floor(bulkBonus + 0.5))
	return luck, speed, bulk
end

function getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
	return getFinalRuneStats()
end

function showToast(text)
	local toast = Instance.new("Frame")
	toast.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
	toast.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 0)
	toast.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 58)
	toast.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 105, 178)
	toast.BorderSizePixel = 0
	toast.Parent = toastHolder
	createCorner(toast, 16)
	createGradient(toast, Color3.fromRGB(105, 162, 255), Color3.fromRGB(72, 101, 177), 0)
	createStroke(toast, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), 2, 0.14)

	local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, 0)
	label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
	label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	label.Text = tostring(text)
	label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	label.TextSize = 22
	label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.25
	label.TextScaled = true
	label.Parent = toast

	TweenService:Create(toast, TweenInfo.new(0.28, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		Size = UDim2.new(0, 420, 0, 58),
		Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, -6)
	}):Play()

	task.spawn(function()
		task.wait(2.2)
		local tweenOut = TweenService:Create(toast, TweenInfo.new(0.42, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
			Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 58),
			Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, -28),
			BackgroundTransparency = 1
		})
		tweenOut:Play()
		tweenOut.Completed:Wait()
		toast:Destroy()
	end)
end

function checkGamepassOwnership(gamepassKey)
	local id = tonumber((GamepassIds or {})[gamepassKey]) or 0
	if id <= 0 then
		return false, "ID не задан"
	end
	local ok, owns = pcall(function()
		return MarketplaceService:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(player.UserId, id)
	end)
	if not ok then
		return false, "Ошибка проверки"
	end
	return owns == true, owns and "Есть" or "Нет"
end

function syncGamepassValue(gamepassKey, owns)
	if gamepassKey == "DoubleCoins" and doubleCoinsGamepass then doubleCoinsGamepass.Value = owns and true or false end
	if gamepassKey == "DoublePaper" and doublePaperGamepass then doublePaperGamepass.Value = owns and true or false end
	if gamepassKey == "DoubleWood" and doubleWoodGamepass then doubleWoodGamepass.Value = owns and true or false end
	if gamepassKey == "TripleRuneLuck" and tripleRuneLuckGamepass then tripleRuneLuckGamepass.Value = owns and true or false end
end

activeAdminEvents = {}
ADMIN_EVENT_UPGRADES = {
	RuneLuckX2 = {runeLuckMul = 2, adminUpgradeLabel = "Luck x2"},
	RuneSpeedX2 = {runeSpeedMul = 2, adminUpgradeLabel = "Speed x2"},
	RuneBulkX5 = {runeBulkMul = 5, adminUpgradeLabel = "Bulk x5"},
	StatsX2 = {adminUpgradeLabel = "Global x2"},
	PassiveLuckX3 = {adminUpgradeLabel = "PassiveLuck x3"},
}
adminEventTitles = {
	StatsX2 = "x2 Stats",
	RuneBulkX5 = "x5 Rune Bulk",
	RuneSpeedX2 = "x2 Rune Speed",
	RuneLuckX2 = "x2 Rune Luck",
	PassiveLuckX3 = "x3 Passive Luck",
}
adminEventDescs = {
	StatsX2 = "Удваивает Coins/Wood/Paper/XP доход.",
	RuneBulkX5 = "Умножает Rune Bulk на x5.",
	RuneSpeedX2 = "Удваивает скорость открытия рун.",
	RuneLuckX2 = "Удваивает Rune Luck.",
	PassiveLuckX3 = "Утрояет шанс редких пассивов.",
}

getActiveAdminEventUpgrades = function()
	local luckMul, speedMul, bulkMul, bulkAdd = 1, 1, 1, 0
	for _, ev in ipairs(activeAdminEvents or {}) do
		local eventData = type(ev) == "table" and ev or {}
		if (tonumber(eventData.timeLeft) or 0) > 0 then
			local cfg = ADMIN_EVENT_UPGRADES[tostring(eventData.key or "")]
			if cfg then
				luckMul *= cfg.runeLuckMul or 1
				speedMul *= cfg.runeSpeedMul or 1
				bulkMul *= cfg.runeBulkMul or 1
				bulkAdd += cfg.runeBulkAdd or 0
			end
		end
	end
	return luckMul, speedMul, bulkMul, bulkAdd
end

function formatAdminEventTime(timeLeft)
	local total = math.max(0, math.floor(tonumber(timeLeft) or 0))
	if total < 60 then
		return tostring(total) .. "с"
	end
	local minutes = math.floor(total / 60)
	local seconds = total % 60
	if minutes < 60 then
		return string.format("%dм %dс", minutes, seconds)
	end
	local hours = math.floor(minutes / 60)
	local remMinutes = minutes % 60
	return string.format("%dч %dм", hours, remMinutes)
end

function renderAdminEvents(events)
	for _, child in ipairs(adminEventGui:GetChildren()) do
		if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
	end
	for _, ev in ipairs(events or {}) do
		local eventData = type(ev) == "table" and ev or {}
		local eventId = tostring(eventData.key or eventData.eventId or eventData["id"] or "unknown")
		local compactAdmin = getDevicePreset() == "PHONE"
		local row = Instance.new("Frame")
		row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, compactAdmin and 34 or 42)
		row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 56, 92)
		row.BorderSizePixel = 0
		row.Parent = adminEventGui
		createCorner(row, 12)
		local eventTheme = ADMIN_EVENT_UPGRADES[eventId] or {}
		local rowColor1 = eventTheme.rowColor1 or Color3.fromRGB(88, 128, 194)
		local rowColor2 = eventTheme.rowColor2 or Color3.fromRGB(36, 52, 90)
		local strokeColor = eventTheme.strokeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		local rowStroke = createStroke(row, strokeColor, 1.6, 0.18)
		pulseStroke(rowStroke, 0.18, 0.38, 1.8)
		createGradient(row, rowColor1, rowColor2, 0)
		createStroke(row, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), 1.1, 0.25)
		local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
		icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, compactAdmin and 22 or 28, 0, compactAdmin and 22 or 28)
		icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, compactAdmin and -11 or -14)
		icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		icon.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.AdminEventIcons[eventId] or "")
		icon.Parent = row
		local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		text.Size = UDim2.new(1, -96, 1, -8)
		text.Position = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 4)
		text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		text.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
		local upgradeLabel = (ADMIN_EVENT_UPGRADES[eventId] and ADMIN_EVENT_UPGRADES[eventId].adminUpgradeLabel) or ""
		local prettyTime = formatAdminEventTime(eventData.timeLeft)
		text.Text = (adminEventTitles[eventId] or eventId) .. (upgradeLabel ~= "" and (" [" .. upgradeLabel .. "]") or "")
		text.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(236, 245, 255)
		text.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		text.TextSize = compactAdmin and 11 or 14
		text.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
		text.Parent = row
		local timer = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		timer.Size = UDim2.new(0, 54, 0, 20)
		timer.Position = UDim2.new(1, -62, 0.5, -10)
		timer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		timer.Text = prettyTime
		timer.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(214, 246, 255)
		timer.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
		timer.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
		timer.TextSize = compactAdmin and 11 or 14
		timer.Parent = row
		local bar = Instance.new("Frame")
		bar.Size = UDim2.new(safeClamp((tonumber(eventData.timeLeft) or 0) / 3600, 0.05, 1), 0, 0, 3)
		bar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 1, -5)
		bar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(162, 236, 255)
		bar.BorderSizePixel = 0
		bar.Parent = row
		row.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
			adminEventTooltip.Visible = true
			adminEventTooltip.Position = UDim2.new(0, 270, 1, -130)
			adminEventTooltip.Text = (adminEventTitles[eventId] or eventId) .. "\n" .. (adminEventDescs[eventId] or eventData.tooltip or "") .. "\nОсталось: " .. formatAdminEventTime(eventData.timeLeft)
		end)
		row.MouseLeave:Connect(function() adminEventTooltip.Visible = false end)
	end
end

function normalizeAdminEvents(rawEvents)
	local normalized = {}
	if type(rawEvents) ~= "table" then
		return normalized
	end
	if #rawEvents > 0 then
		for idx = 1, #rawEvents do
			local ev = rawEvents[idx]
			if type(ev) == "table" then
				local key = tostring(ev.key or ev.eventId or "")
				local left = tonumber(ev.timeLeft or ev.remaining or ev.left) or 0
				if key ~= "" and left > 0 then
					normalized[#normalized + 1] = {
						key = key,
						timeLeft = left,
						tooltip = adminEventDescs[key] or tostring(ev.tooltip or ""),
					}
				end
			end
		end
	else
		for key, remain in pairs(rawEvents) do
			local left = tonumber(remain) or 0
			local keyText = tostring(key)
			if keyText ~= "" and left > 0 then
				normalized[#normalized + 1] = {
					key = keyText,
					timeLeft = left,
					tooltip = adminEventDescs[keyText] or "",
				}
			end
		end
	end
	return normalized
end

function showPickup(iconKey, amount)
	amount = tonumber(amount) or 0
	local holder = Instance.new("Frame")
	holder.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	activePickupCount += 1
	local stackIndex = math.min(activePickupCount - 1, 5)
	holder.Position = UDim2.new(0.5 + math.random(-8, 8) / 100, 0, 0.72 - (stackIndex * 0.055), 0)
	holder.Size = UDim2.new(0, 146, 0, 52)
	holder.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	holder.Parent = pickupLayer

	local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 38)
	icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -19)
	icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	icon.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
	local notifyIcon = AssetSlots.NotificationIcons[iconKey] or AssetSlots.NotificationIcons.Coin
	icon.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(notifyIcon)
	icon.Parent = holder

	local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	text.Position = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 4)
	text.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 44)
	text.Text = "+" .. formatNumber(amount)
	text.TextColor3 = iconKey == "Tree" and Color3.fromRGB(207, 255, 183) or iconKey == "Paper" and Color3.fromRGB(230, 235, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 239, 126)
	text.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	text.TextScaled = true
	text.Parent = holder

	local move = TweenService:Create(holder, TweenInfo.new(0.6, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		Position = holder.Position - UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.08, 0)
	})
	local fade = TweenService:Create(text, TweenInfo.new(0.9), {TextTransparency = 1})
	local pulse = TweenService:Create(icon, TweenInfo.new(0.25), {ImageTransparency = 0.15, Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 42)})
	move:Play()
	fade:Play()
	pulse:Play()
	task.delay(1, function()
		activePickupCount = math.max(0, activePickupCount - 1)
		holder:Destroy()
	end)
end

function setButtonVisual(button, text, canBuy, atMax, activeColor, disabledColor, textColor, locked)
	if not button then
		return
	end
	button.Active = true
	button.Selectable = true
	if locked then
		button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(74, 82, 78)
		button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 244, 255)
		button.Text = "LOCKED"
		button.AutoButtonColor = false
		button.Active = false
		button.Selectable = false
		return
	end

	if atMax then
		button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(96, 164, 96)
		button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(232, 255, 229)
		button.Text = "MAX"
		button.AutoButtonColor = false
		button.Active = false
		button.Selectable = false
		return
	end

	if canBuy then
		button.BackgroundColor3 = activeColor
		button.TextColor3 = textColor
		button.AutoButtonColor = true
	else
		button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(126, 62, 62)
		button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 220, 220)
		button.AutoButtonColor = false
	end

	button.Text = text
end

function spawnCoin(layer, progress)
	local coin = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	local size = math.random(ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.minCoinSize, ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.maxCoinSize)
	coin.Size = UDim2.new(0, size, 0, size)
	coin.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	coin.Position = UDim2.new(math.random(), 0, -0.2 - math.random() * 0.25, 0)
	coin.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	coin.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(ICON_ASSET_IDS.CurrencyCoin)
	coin.ImageTransparency = 0.08 + math.random() * 0.28
	coin.Rotation = math.random(-30, 30)
	coin.ZIndex = 95 + math.random(0, 8)
	coin.Parent = layer

	local targetY = safeClamp(0.35 + progress * 0.72 + math.random() * 0.18, 0.35, 1.12)
	local targetX = safeClamp(coin.Position.X.Scale + ((math.random() - 0.5) * 0.08), 0.02, 0.98)
	local tween = TweenService:Create(coin, TweenInfo.new(1.7 + math.random() * 1.9, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
		Position = UDim2.new(targetX, 0, targetY, 0),
		Rotation = coin.Rotation + math.random(-160, 160),
	})
	tween:Play()

	if math.random() > 0.55 then
		task.spawn(function()
			for _ = 1, 2 do
				if not coin.Parent then break end
				TweenService:Create(coin, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
					Position = coin.Position + UDim2.new((math.random() - 0.5) * 0.03, 0, 0, 0),
				}):Play()
				task.wait(0.25)
			end
		end)
	end
	return coin
end

function showReward(layer, passiveName, passiveIcon, rarityColor, onClose)
	local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
	frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 420, 0, 210)
	frame.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.52, 0)
	frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(44, 57, 92)
	frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	frame.ZIndex = 140
	frame.Parent = layer
	createCorner(frame, 18)
	createStroke(frame, rarityColor, 3, 0.05)
	createGradient(frame, Color3.fromRGB(88, 114, 176), Color3.fromRGB(42, 53, 90), 90)

	local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 108, 0, 108)
	icon.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
	icon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 20)
	icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	icon.Image = passiveIcon
	icon.ZIndex = 141
	icon.Parent = frame

	local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 58)
	label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 1, -70)
	label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	label.Text = passiveName
	label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 247, 197)
	label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	label.TextScaled = true
	label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.45
	label.ZIndex = 141
	label.Parent = frame

	local scale = Instance.new("UIScale")
	scale.Scale = 0.72
	scale.Parent = frame
	TweenService:Create(frame, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.04}):Play()
	TweenService:Create(scale, TweenInfo.new(0.36, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Scale = 1}):Play()

	local closeBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
	closeBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
	closeBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -17, 1, 8)
	closeBtn.Text = "✕"
	closeBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
	closeBtn.TextScaled = true
	closeBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	closeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 122, 122)
	closeBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
	closeBtn.ZIndex = 145
	closeBtn.Parent = frame
	createCorner(closeBtn, 999)
	closeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if onClose then
			onClose()
		end
	end)
	return frame
end

function cleanupAnimation(layer, dimmer, coins, rewardFrame)
	local fadeInfo = TweenInfo.new(ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.fadeOutTime)
	TweenService:Create(dimmer, fadeInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
	if rewardFrame then
		TweenService:Create(rewardFrame, fadeInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
	end
	for _, coin in ipairs(coins) do
		if coin and coin.Parent then
			TweenService:Create(coin, fadeInfo, {ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
		end
	end
	task.wait(ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.fadeOutTime + 0.05)
	layer.Visible = false
	for _, c in ipairs(layer:GetChildren()) do
		c:Destroy()
	end
	isRovRolling = false
end

function startRollAnimation(passiveName, passiveIcon, rarityColor)
	if not passiveUi.rollFxLayer then return end
	isRovRolling = true
	for _, c in ipairs(passiveUi.rollFxLayer:GetChildren()) do
		c:Destroy()
	end
	passiveUi.rollFxLayer.Visible = true

	local dimmer = Instance.new("Frame")
	dimmer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	dimmer.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(8, 14, 28)
	dimmer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	dimmer.ZIndex = 91
	dimmer.Parent = passiveUi.rollFxLayer
	TweenService:Create(dimmer, TweenInfo.new(0.8), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.28}):Play()

	local coinLayer = Instance.new("Frame")
	coinLayer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	coinLayer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	coinLayer.ZIndex = 93
	coinLayer.Parent = passiveUi.rollFxLayer

	local coins = {}
	task.spawn(function()
		local elapsed = 0
		local rewardFrame = nil
		local closeRequested = false
		while elapsed < ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.duration do
			local progress = safeClamp(elapsed / ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.duration, 0, 1)
			table.insert(coins, spawnCoin(coinLayer, progress))
			if elapsed >= ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.rewardRevealTime and not rewardFrame then
				rewardFrame = showReward(passiveUi.rollFxLayer, passiveName, passiveIcon, rarityColor, function()
					closeRequested = true
				end)
			end
			if closeRequested then
				break
			end
			elapsed += ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.coinSpawnInterval
			task.wait(ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.coinSpawnInterval)
		end
		while #coins < ROLL_ANIMATION_CONFIG.totalCoins do
			table.insert(coins, spawnCoin(coinLayer, 1))
		end
		cleanupAnimation(passiveUi.rollFxLayer, dimmer, coins, rewardFrame)
	end)
end

function playRovAnimation(passiveDef)
	local name = passiveDef and passiveDef.name or "Новый пассив"
	local passiveId = passiveDef and passiveDef["id"]
	local icon = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.PassiveIcons[passiveId] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.PassiveCardDefault)
	local rarityColor = getRarityColor(passiveDef and passiveDef.rarity or "Common")
	startRollAnimation(name, icon, rarityColor)
end

function formatCostWithCurrency(costValue, currencyName)
	local label = tostring(currencyName or "")
	if label == "" then
		return formatNumber(costValue)
	end
	return formatNumber(costValue) .. " " .. label
end

function updateCard(card, levelValue, costValue, activeValue, maxLevel, currentCurrency, lockedReason, currencyName)
	if not card or not card.levelLabel or not card.costLabel or not card.statusLabel or not card.buyButton or not card.maxButton then
		return
	end
	local locked = lockedReason ~= nil
	local atMax = (not locked) and maxLevel ~= math.huge and levelValue >= maxLevel
	local canBuy = (not locked) and (not atMax) and costValue > 0 and currentCurrency >= costValue
	local shownCurrency = currencyName or card.currencyName or ""

	if maxLevel == math.huge then
		card.levelLabel.Text = "Lv " .. tostring(levelValue) .. "/∞"
	else
		card.levelLabel.Text = "Lv " .. tostring(levelValue) .. "/" .. tostring(maxLevel)
	end

	if locked then
		card.costLabel.Text = "Cost: LOCKED"
		card.statusLabel.Text = lockedReason
	elseif atMax then
		card.costLabel.Text = "Cost: MAX"
		card.statusLabel.Text = "Completed"
	else
		card.costLabel.Text = "Cost: " .. formatCostWithCurrency(costValue, shownCurrency)
		card.statusLabel.Text = activeValue and "Active upgrade" or "Inactive"
	end

	setButtonVisual(card.buyButton, "Buy", canBuy, atMax, card.buttonActive or Color3.fromRGB(99, 243, 200), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), card.buttonText or Color3.fromRGB(22, 48, 62), locked)
	setButtonVisual(card.maxButton, "Buy Max", canBuy, atMax, card.buttonMax or Color3.fromRGB(177, 122, 255), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), card.buttonText or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), locked)
end

function getPaperCycleTime()
	local value = 10 - (paperSpeedLevel.Value * 0.5)
	if value < 5 then
		value = 5
	end
	return roundToTenth(value)
end

function getPaperProductionAmount()
	local baseValue = 1 + paperValueLevel.Value
	local multiplier = 1 + (paperMultiplierLevel.Value * 0.1)
	return roundToTenth(baseValue * multiplier)
end

wallParts = {}
if rebirthWall:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(wallParts, rebirthWall)
end
for _, obj in ipairs(rebirthWall:GetDescendants()) do
	if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
		table.insert(wallParts, obj)
	end
end

function isSystemUnlocked(stage)
	if stage == 2 then return secondAreaUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 2 end
	if stage == 3 then return thirdUpgradeUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 3 end
	if stage == 4 then return fourthSystemsUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 4 end
	if stage == 5 then return fifthSystemsUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 5 end
	if stage == 6 then return sixthSystemsUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 6 end
	return false
end

function setCardVisible(cardObj, visible)
	if not cardObj then return end
	if cardObj.card then
		cardObj.card.Visible = visible
	end
	if cardObj.buyButton then
		cardObj.buyButton.Visible = visible
		cardObj.buyButton.Active = visible
	end
	if cardObj.maxButton then
		cardObj.maxButton.Visible = visible
		cardObj.maxButton.Active = visible
	end
end

function updateWallVisual()
	for _, part in ipairs(wallParts) do
		part.LocalTransparencyModifier = secondAreaUnlocked.Value and 0.78 or 0
	end
end

updateBoards = function()
	local secondUnlockedVisual = secondAreaUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 2
	local thirdUnlockedVisual = thirdUpgradeUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 3
	local fourthUnlockedVisual = fourthSystemsUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 4
	local fifthUnlockedVisual = fifthSystemsUnlocked.Value or rebirthCount.Value >= 5
	local seventhUnlockedVisual = rebirthCount.Value >= 7

	function setWorldNodeVisible(node, visible)
		if not node then return end
		if node:IsA("BasePart") then
			if node:GetAttribute("OrigTransparency") == nil then
				node:SetAttribute("OrigTransparency", node.Transparency)
				node:SetAttribute("OrigCanCollide", node.CanCollide)
				node:SetAttribute("OrigCanTouch", node.CanTouch)
				node:SetAttribute("OrigCanQuery", node.CanQuery)
			end
			node.Transparency = visible and (node:GetAttribute("OrigTransparency") or 0) or 1
			node.CanCollide = visible and (node:GetAttribute("OrigCanCollide") ~= false) or false
			node.CanTouch = visible and (node:GetAttribute("OrigCanTouch") ~= false) or false
			node.CanQuery = visible and (node:GetAttribute("OrigCanQuery") ~= false) or false
			for _, c in ipairs(node:GetDescendants()) do
				if c:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or c:IsA("Beam") or c:IsA("Trail") then
					c.Enabled = visible
				elseif c:IsA("PointLight") or c:IsA("SpotLight") or c:IsA("SurfaceLight") then
					c.Enabled = visible
				elseif c:IsA("Highlight") then
					c.Enabled = visible
				elseif c:IsA("BillboardGui") or c:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
					c.Enabled = visible
					c.Active = visible
				end
			end
		elseif node:IsA("Model") then
			for _, d in ipairs(node:GetDescendants()) do
				if d:IsA("BasePart") then
					if d:GetAttribute("OrigTransparency") == nil then
						d:SetAttribute("OrigTransparency", d.Transparency)
						d:SetAttribute("OrigCanCollide", d.CanCollide)
						d:SetAttribute("OrigCanTouch", d.CanTouch)
						d:SetAttribute("OrigCanQuery", d.CanQuery)
					end
					d.Transparency = visible and (d:GetAttribute("OrigTransparency") or 0) or 1
					d.CanCollide = visible and (d:GetAttribute("OrigCanCollide") ~= false) or false
					d.CanTouch = visible and (d:GetAttribute("OrigCanTouch") ~= false) or false
					d.CanQuery = visible and (d:GetAttribute("OrigCanQuery") ~= false) or false
				elseif d:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or d:IsA("Beam") or d:IsA("Trail") then
					d.Enabled = visible
				elseif d:IsA("PointLight") or d:IsA("SpotLight") or d:IsA("SurfaceLight") then
					d.Enabled = visible
				elseif d:IsA("Highlight") then
					d.Enabled = visible
				elseif d:IsA("BillboardGui") or d:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
					d.Enabled = visible
					d.Active = visible
				end
			end
		end
	end

	setWorldNodeVisible(treeBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(treeDoska, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(treeUpgradeDoska, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(paperFactoryDoska, fourthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(paperUpgradeDoska, fourthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(passiveRollBlock, fifthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(passiveInventoryBlock, fifthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(runeRollBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(runeIndexBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(runeStatsIndexBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(runeUpgradeBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(runeUpgradeDoska, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(xpUpgradeDoska, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(xpProgressDoska, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(forestRuneBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(forestRuneIndexBoard, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(forestRuneStatsBoard, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(natureRuneBlock, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(natureRuneIndexBoard, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(natureRuneStatsBoard, secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(hayBlock, seventhUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(hayIndexBoardPart, seventhUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(hayUpgradeBoardPart, seventhUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldNodeVisible(hayAreaGate, not seventhUnlockedVisual)

	function setWorldBoardGuiVisible(guiName, visible)
		local gui = playerGui:FindFirstChild(guiName)
		if gui and gui:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
			gui.Enabled = visible
			gui.Active = visible
		end
	end
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("CoinsBoardSurfaceGui", true)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("UpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", true)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("RebirthBoardSurfaceGui", true)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("TreeBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("TreeUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("BoostBoardSurfaceGui", fourthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("PaperFactoryBoardSurfaceGui", fourthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("PaperUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", fourthUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("RuneUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("XPUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("XPProgressBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("RuneIndexBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("RuneStatsIndexBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("NatureRuneIndexBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("NatureRuneStatsBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("ForestRuneIndexBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("ForestRuneStatsBoardSurfaceGui", secondUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("HayIndexBoardSurfaceGui", seventhUnlockedVisual)
	setWorldBoardGuiVisible("HayUpgradeBoardSurfaceGui", seventhUnlockedVisual)

	function updateUnlockDebug()
		-- debug panel removed in production build


		local coinGoalBoostMultiplier = fourthUnlockedVisual and select(1, computeGoalWoodFactor(coins.Value)) or 1
		coinValueLabel.Text = formatNumber(coins.Value)
		coinRewardLabel.Text = formatNumber(getCoinReward())
		xpValueLabel.Text = formatNumber(xpValue.Value)
		coinUpgradeMultiplierLabel.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(getCoinUpgradeMultiplier())
		coinRebirthMultiplierLabel.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(rebirthCoinMultiplierBonus.Value)
		coinGoalBoostLabel.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(coinGoalBoostMultiplier)
		coinRespawnLabel.Text = formatNumber(getCoinRespawn()) .. "s"
		if adminCoinChainLabel then
			adminCoinChainLabel.Text = "Coin chain: base x" .. formatNumber(1 + coinValueLevel.Value)
				.. " * upgrade x" .. formatNumber(getCoinUpgradeMultiplier())
				.. " * rebirth x" .. formatNumber(rebirthCoinMultiplierBonus.Value)
				.. " * CoinGoal x" .. formatNumber(coinGoalBoostMultiplier)
				.. " => " .. formatNumber(getCoinReward())
		end
		rebirthCountLabel.Text = tostring(rebirthCount.Value)

		setCardVisible(coinWoodBoostCard, thirdUnlockedVisual)
		setCardVisible(treeCoinBoostCard, thirdUnlockedVisual)
		if paperUpgradeCards then
			setCardVisible(paperUpgradeCards.gain, fourthUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(paperUpgradeCards.multi, fourthUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(paperUpgradeCards.speed, fourthUnlockedVisual)
		end
		if xpUpgradeCards then
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.coin, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.wood, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.paper, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.xpMul, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.runeLuck, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.runeBulk, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(xpUpgradeCards.runeSpeed, secondUnlockedVisual)
		end
		if runeUpgradeCards then
			setCardVisible(runeUpgradeCards.luck, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(runeUpgradeCards.speed, secondUnlockedVisual)
			setCardVisible(runeUpgradeCards.bulk, secondUnlockedVisual)
		end

		updateCard(coinGainCard, coinValueLevel.Value, coinValueCost.Value, coinValueActive.Value, math.huge, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
		updateCard(coinMultiCard, coinMultiplierLevel.Value, coinMultiplierCost.Value, coinMultiplierActive.Value, math.huge, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
		updateCard(coinSpawnCard, coinSpawnLevel.Value, coinSpawnCost.Value, coinSpawnActive.Value, MAX_COIN_SPAWN_SPEED_LEVEL, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
		updateCard(
			coinWoodBoostCard,
			coinWoodBoostLevel.Value,
			coinWoodBoostCost.Value,
			coinWoodBoostActive.Value,
			10,
			coins.Value,
			nil,
			"Coins"
		)

		rebirthLevelText.Text = "Rebirth " .. tostring(rebirthCount.Value) .. "/" .. tostring(MAX_REBIRTH_COUNT)
		rebirthCurrentText.Text = "Сейчас: x" .. formatNumber(rebirthCoinMultiplierBonus.Value) .. " | Goal x" .. formatNumber(coinGoalBoostMultiplier) .. " | -" .. formatNumber(rebirthSpawnSpeedBonus.Value) .. "с"

		if rebirthCount.Value == 0 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "1-е: x2 монеты и -0.1с к спавну"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 1 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "2-е: x5 поверх и открытие дерева"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 2 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "3-е: x10 монет и новые апгрейды"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 3 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "4-е: x2 дерево, буст-доска, бумага"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 4 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "5-е: пассивы и инвентарь (50 бумаги)"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 5 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "6-е: руны, индекс, ускорение рунной прогрессии"
		elseif rebirthCount.Value == 6 then
			rebirthNextText.Text = "7-е: Hay, HayBlock, HayBoard, HayAreaGate, +50% Rune Luck"
		else
			rebirthNextText.Text = "Все перерождения куплены"
		end

		rebirthUnlockText.Text = secondUnlockedVisual and "Новая зона: открыта" or "Новая зона: закрыта"

		local rebirthAtMax = rebirthNextCost.Value <= 0
		local currencyLabel = rebirthNextCurrency.Value ~= "None" and rebirthNextCurrency.Value or ""
		local rebirthCanBuy = false
		if not rebirthAtMax then
			if currencyLabel == "Coins" then
				rebirthCanBuy = coins.Value >= rebirthNextCost.Value
			elseif currencyLabel == "Wood" then
				rebirthCanBuy = woodCurrency.Value >= rebirthNextCost.Value
			elseif currencyLabel == "Paper" then
				rebirthCanBuy = paperValue.Value >= rebirthNextCost.Value
			end
		end

		if rebirthAtMax then
			rebirthCostText.Text = "Cost: MAX"
		else
			rebirthCostText.Text = "Cost: " .. formatNumber(rebirthNextCost.Value) .. " " .. currencyLabel
		end

		setButtonVisual(rebirthButton, "REBIRTH!", rebirthCanBuy, rebirthAtMax, Color3.fromRGB(255, 218, 96), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(65, 46, 93))

		treeCurrencyText.Text = formatNumber(woodCurrency.Value)
		treeRewardText.Text = formatNumber(getWoodReward())
		treeMultiplierText.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(1 + woodMultiplierLevel.Value + (coinWoodBoostLevel.Value * 0.25))
		treeCooldownText.Text = formatNumber(getWoodCooldown()) .. "s"
		treeUnlockStatusText.Text = secondUnlockedVisual and "Открыто" or "Закрыто"

		updateCard(treeGainCard, woodValueLevel.Value, woodValueCost.Value, woodValueActive.Value, math.huge, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
		updateCard(treeMultiCard, woodMultiplierLevel.Value, woodMultiplierCost.Value, woodMultiplierActive.Value, math.huge, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
		updateCard(treeSpeedCard, woodSpeedLevel.Value, woodSpeedCost.Value, woodSpeedActive.Value, math.huge, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
		updateCard(
			treeCoinBoostCard,
			woodCoinBoostLevel.Value,
			woodCoinBoostCost.Value,
			woodCoinBoostActive.Value,
			20,
			woodCurrency.Value,
			nil,
			"Wood"
		)

		local goalFactor, goalsReached, nextTarget = computeGoalWoodFactor(coins.Value)
		boostFactorText.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(goalFactor)
		boostGoalsText.Text = formatNumber(goalsReached)
		boostNextTargetText.Text = goalFactor >= 10 and "MAX" or formatNumber(nextTarget)
		boostCoinText.Text = formatNumber(coins.Value)

		paperText.Text = formatNumber(paperValue.Value)
		fuelText.Text = formatNumber(fuelValue.Value)
		countdownText.Text = formatNumber(factoryCountdown.Value) .. "s"
		factoryStatusText.Text = factoryRunning.Value and "Работает" or "Нет топлива"
		paperProductionText.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(getPaperProductionAmount())
		local cycleTime = getPaperCycleTime()
		local progress = 0
		if factoryRunning.Value and cycleTime > 0 then
			progress = safeClamp(1 - (factoryCountdown.Value / cycleTime), 0, 1)
		end
		-- production progress bar removed for cleaner paper factory layout

		if paperUpgradeCards then
			updateCard(paperUpgradeCards.gain, paperValueLevel.Value, paperValueCost.Value, paperValueActive.Value, math.huge, paperValue.Value, nil, "Paper")
			updateCard(paperUpgradeCards.multi, paperMultiplierLevel.Value, paperMultiplierCost.Value, paperMultiplierActive.Value, math.huge, paperValue.Value, nil, "Paper")
			updateCard(paperUpgradeCards.speed, paperSpeedLevel.Value, paperSpeedCost.Value, paperSpeedActive.Value, 10, paperValue.Value, nil, "Paper")
			if paperUpgradeLockedOverlay then
				paperUpgradeLockedOverlay.Visible = false
			end
		end

		treeInfoLockedOverlay.Visible = false
		treeUpgradeLockedOverlay.Visible = false
		boostLockedOverlay.Visible = false
		factoryLockedOverlay.Visible = false

		if passiveUi.indexPanel then passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible = fifthUnlockedVisual and passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible or false end
		if passiveUi.inventoryPanel then passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible = fifthUnlockedVisual and passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible or false end
		if runeUi.panel and not secondUnlockedVisual then runeUi.panel.Visible = false end
		if runeUi.sessionPanel and not secondUnlockedVisual then runeUi.sessionPanel.Visible = false end
		if xpProgressUi and xpProgressUi.panel then xpProgressUi.panel.Visible = secondUnlockedVisual end

		if passiveUi.hintGui then
			passiveUi.hintGui.Enabled = fifthUnlockedVisual
		end
		local passiveInventory = {}
		if passiveUi.inventoryPanel then
			local state = parsePassiveState()
			passiveInventory = (state and state.inventory) or {}
			passiveUi.lastState = state
			local renderSignature = passiveStateJson.Value .. "|" .. tostring(passiveUi.selectedUid or "") .. "|" .. tostring(fifthUnlockedVisual) .. "|" .. tostring(math.floor(paperValue.Value + 0.5))
			if passiveUi.lastRenderSignature ~= renderSignature then
				passiveUi.lastRenderSignature = renderSignature
				local equippedName = "none"
				local inventoryProfile = getDeviceProfile()
				local mobileInventory = inventoryProfile == "mobile"
				local compactInventory = inventoryProfile == "mobile" or inventoryProfile == "tablet"
				for _, child in ipairs(passiveUi.slotsList:GetChildren()) do
					if child:IsA("TextButton") then
						child:Destroy()
					end
				end
			end
			for _, entry in ipairs(passiveInventory) do
				if type(entry) == "table" and entry.passiveId and entry.uid then
					local def = PASSIVE_DEFS[entry.passiveId]
					if def then
						local b = Instance.new("TextButton")
						local isEquipped = entry.uid == state.equippedUid
						local isSelected = entry.uid == passiveUi.selectedUid
						b.Size = UDim2.new(0, mobileInventory and 95 or (compactInventory and 110 or 132), 0, mobileInventory and 95 or (compactInventory and 110 or 112))
						b.Text = ""
						b.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 16, 22)
						b.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
						b.BorderSizePixel = 0
						b.Parent = passiveUi.slotsList
						createCorner(b, 10)
						local customBg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
						customBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
						customBg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						customBg.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.PassiveInventoryBackgrounds[entry.passiveId])
						customBg.ImageTransparency = customBg.Image == "" and 1 or 0
						customBg.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Crop
						customBg.Parent = b
						local c1, c2, c3 = getPassiveStyle(entry.passiveId, def.rarity)
						b.BackgroundColor3 = c1
						-- no forced default tint; visuals come from direct image background + border style
						local edgeColor = isEquipped and Color3.fromRGB(206, 255, 192) or getRarityColor(def.rarity)
						local edge = createStroke(b, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), isEquipped and 3 or 2.4, isSelected and 0.01 or 0.07)
						pulseStroke(edge, isSelected and 0.01 or 0.07, def.rarity == "Common" and 0.2 or 0.34, def.rarity == "Mythic" and 0.85 or 1.6)
						createStroke(b, edgeColor, 1.2, 0.2)
						createGradient(b, c1, c3, 40)
						decorateCardCorners(b)
						if def.rarity == "Mythic" or def.rarity == "Secret" then
							local mythicGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
							mythicGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
								ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 95, 172)),
								ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.33, Color3.fromRGB(101, 196, 255)),
								ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.66, Color3.fromRGB(158, 255, 126)),
								ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 212, 108)),
							})
							mythicGradient.Parent = edge
						end
						-- Stable hover/click: no scale teleporting.
						local spark = Instance.new("TextLabel")
						spark.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						spark.Size = UDim2.new(0, 28, 0, 18)
						spark.Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0, 4)
						spark.Text = def.rarity == "Mythic" and "✦✦" or (def.rarity == "Legendary" and "✦" or "")
						spark.TextColor3 = getRarityColor(def.rarity)
						spark.TextScaled = true
						spark.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
						spark.Parent = b
						local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
						icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, mobileInventory and 54 or (compactInventory and 64 or 72), 0, mobileInventory and 54 or (compactInventory and 64 or 72))
						icon.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
						icon.Position = compactInventory and UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, mobileInventory and 10 or 12) or UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 8)
						icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						icon.Image = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.PassiveCardImages[entry.passiveId] or ICON_ASSET_IDS.PassiveCardDefault)
						icon.Parent = b
						local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
						title.Size = UDim2.new(1, compactInventory and -8 or -90, 0, compactInventory and 22 or 28)
						title.Position = compactInventory and UDim2.new(0, 4, 1, mobileInventory and -26 or -28) or UDim2.new(0, 84, 0, 8)
						title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						title.TextXAlignment = compactInventory and Enum.TextXAlignment.Center or Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
						title.TextScaled = false
						title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
						title.TextSize = mobileInventory and 12 or (compactInventory and 14 or 18)
						title.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 250, 255)
						title.Text = ""
						title.Visible = false
						title.Parent = b
						local info = Instance.new("TextLabel")
						info.Size = UDim2.new(1, mobileInventory and -90 or -90, 0, mobileInventory and 48 or 40)
						info.Position = UDim2.new(0, mobileInventory and 84 or 84, 0, mobileInventory and 44 or 34)
						info.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						info.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
						info.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
						info.TextWrapped = true
						info.TextScaled = true
						info.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
						info.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(228, 236, 255)
						info.Text = ""
						info.Visible = false
						info.Parent = b
						local status = Instance.new("TextLabel")
						status.Size = UDim2.new(1, mobileInventory and -90 or -90, 0, mobileInventory and 24 or 20)
						status.Position = UDim2.new(0, mobileInventory and 84 or 84, 1, mobileInventory and -52 or -46)
						status.BackgroundTransparency = 1
						status.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
						status.TextScaled = true
						status.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
						status.TextColor3 = isEquipped and Color3.fromRGB(198, 255, 190) or Color3.fromRGB(225, 235, 255)
						status.Text = isEquipped and "Экипировано" or "Не экипировано"
						status.Visible = not compactInventory
						status.Parent = b
						local effectBadge = Instance.new("TextLabel")
						effectBadge.Size = UDim2.new(0, mobileInventory and 210 or 180, 0, mobileInventory and 26 or 20)
						effectBadge.Position = UDim2.new(1, mobileInventory and -218 or -186, 1, mobileInventory and -30 or -24)
						effectBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(23, 28, 40)
						effectBadge.TextColor3 = edgeColor
						effectBadge.BorderSizePixel = 0
						effectBadge.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
						effectBadge.TextScaled = true
						effectBadge.Text = ""
						effectBadge.Visible = false
						effectBadge.Parent = b
						createCorner(effectBadge, 8)
						b.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
							passiveUi.selectedUid = entry.uid
							passiveUi.manageTitle.Text = def.name
							if compactInventory then
								passiveUi.manageInfo.Text = "Редкость: " .. tostring(def.rarity or "Common")
									.. "\nШанс: " .. tostring(def.chance or "?")
									.. "\nЭффект: " .. tostring(def.effect or "—")
							else
								passiveUi.manageInfo.Text = "Тип: " .. tostring(def.currencyType or "Coins")
									.. "\nРедкость: " .. tostring(def.rarity or "Common")
									.. "\nШанс: " .. tostring(def.chance or "?")
									.. "\nЭффект: " .. tostring(def.effect or "—")
									.. "\n\n" .. tostring(def.desc or "")
							end
						end)
						if isEquipped then
							equippedName = def.name
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end

		do
			local rs = parseRuneState()
			local natureCounts = rs.natureCounts or rs.counts or {}
			local forestCounts = rs.forestCounts or {}
			for systemId, bundle in pairs(runeSystemBoards or {}) do
				local counts = systemId == "Forest" and forestCounts or natureCounts
				local cfg = RUNE_SYSTEM_UI_CONFIG[systemId]
				if bundle.index and bundle.index.rows and cfg then
					for _, runeId in ipairs(cfg.displayOrder) do
						local label = bundle.index.rows[runeId]
						if label then
							local count = tonumber(counts[runeId]) or 0
							local info = RUNE_EFFECT_INFO[runeId] or RUNE_EFFECT_INFO.Grass
							local capMul = (info.cap or 10)
							local eff = math.min(math.floor((capMul / math.max(info.base, 0.0001)) + 0.5), count)
							local total = eff * info.base
							local baseDenom = tonumber((effectiveRuneDenominators or {})[runeId]) or tonumber(RUNE_VISUALS[runeId] and RUNE_VISUALS[runeId].baseDenominator) or 1
							local finalLuck = select(1, getFinalRuneStats())
							local denom = math.max(1, math.floor((baseDenom / math.max(1, finalLuck)) + 0.5))
							local chance = "1 / " .. tostring(denom)
							local runtime = string.format("Количество: %s\nШанс: %s\nСуммарно: +%.2fx %s", formatNumber(count), chance, total, info.target)
							label:SetAttribute("RuntimeText", runtime)
							label.Text = string.format("%s\n%s\nЗа 1: %s | cap x%.1f", tostring(cfg.names[runeId] or runeId), runtime, info.per, capMul)
						end
					end
				end
				if bundle.stats and bundle.stats.luck then
					local effLuck, effSpeed, effBulk = getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
					local speedOverflowBulk = getRuneSpeedOverflowBulk(effSpeed)
					local effBulkBonus = math.max(0, effBulk - 1)
					local speedSeconds = getRuneRollIntervalFromSpeed(effSpeed)
					bundle.stats.luck.Text = formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x"
					bundle.stats.bulk.Text = "+" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
					bundle.stats.speed.Text = string.format("%ss/roll | Overflow Bulk +%s", formatRuneStatValue(speedSeconds), formatRuneStatValue(speedOverflowBulk))
					bundle.stats.total.Text = "Luck " .. formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x | Speed " .. formatRuneStatValue(effSpeed) .. "x | Bulk +" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
				end
			end
			if not selectedStillExists then
				passiveUi.selectedUid = ""
				passiveUi.manageTitle.Text = "Выбери пассив"
				passiveUi.manageInfo.Text = "Нажми слева на пассив"
			end
			passiveUi.emptyState.Visible = #passiveInventory == 0
			passiveUi.equippedText.Text = "EQUIPPED: " .. string.upper(tostring(equippedName))
		end
		if passiveUi.rollButton then
			setButtonVisual(passiveUi.rollButton, "ROLL PASSIVE (50 Paper)", paperValue.Value >= PASSIVE_ROLL_COST and #passiveInventory < PASSIVE_INVENTORY_CAPACITY and fifthUnlockedVisual, false, Color3.fromRGB(255, 216, 120), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(48, 55, 71), not fifthUnlockedVisual)
		end
		if passiveUi.rollButtonInventory then
			setButtonVisual(passiveUi.rollButtonInventory, "ROLL PASSIVE (50 Paper)", paperValue.Value >= PASSIVE_ROLL_COST and #passiveInventory < PASSIVE_INVENTORY_CAPACITY and fifthUnlockedVisual, false, Color3.fromRGB(255, 216, 120), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(48, 55, 71), not fifthUnlockedVisual)
		end
	end

	do
		local runeUnlocked = secondUnlockedVisual
		if runeUi.panel and runeUi.panel.Visible and not runeUnlocked then
			runeUi.panel.Visible = false
		end
		if runeUi.sessionPanel then
			runeUi.sessionPanel.Visible = runeUnlocked and runeRollingActive
		end
		local rs = parseRuneState()
		local c = rs.counts or {}
		function stacks(v)
			return math.min(10, tonumber(v) or 0)
		end
		local effLuck, effSpeed, effBulk = getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
		if runeUi.indexText then
			runeUi.indexText.Text = "Трава: " .. formatNumber(c.Grass or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Grass)) .. ")\n"
				.. "Тёмная трава: " .. formatNumber(c.DarkGrass or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.DarkGrass)) .. ")\n"
				.. "Одуванчик: " .. formatNumber(c.Dandelion or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Dandelion)) .. ")\n"
				.. "Цветок: " .. formatNumber(c.Flower or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Flower)) .. ")\n"
				.. "Фиалка: " .. formatNumber(c.Violet or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Violet)) .. ")\n"
				.. "Роза: " .. formatNumber(c.Rose or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Rose)) .. ")\n\n"
				.. "Luck x" .. formatNumber(effLuck) .. " | Speed x" .. formatNumber(effSpeed) .. " | Bulk +" .. formatNumber(math.max(0, effBulk - 1))
		end
		if runeUi.openBtn then
			setButtonVisual(runeUi.openBtn, "ОТКРЫТЬ FOREST RUNE (50 Coins)", coins.Value >= 50 and runeUnlocked, false, Color3.fromRGB(151, 227, 184), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(22, 56, 41), not runeUnlocked)
		end
		if runeUi.luckBtn then runeUi.luckBtn.Text = "Luck (" .. tostring(runeLuckCost.Value) .. " C)" end
		if runeUi.speedBtn then runeUi.speedBtn.Text = "Speed (" .. tostring(runeSpeedCost.Value) .. " W)" end
		if runeUi.bulkBtn then runeUi.bulkBtn.Text = "Bulk (" .. tostring(runeBulkCost.Value) .. " P)" end
		refreshRuneStats()
		local safeHayState = buildStableHaySnapshot()
		local hayAmountLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayAmount")
		local hayMultiplierLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayMultiplier")
		local hayCooldownLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayCooldown")
		local hayCurrencyValue = tonumber(type(safeHayState) == "table" and safeHayState.HayCurrency or 0) or 0
		if hayUiRows.gain then
			local gain = (1 + hayAmountLevelValue) * (1 + hayMultiplierLevelValue * 0.5)
			local cooldown = math.max(0.8, 5 - hayCooldownLevelValue * 0.1)
			hayUiRows.currency.Text = formatNumber(hayCurrencyValue)
			hayUiRows.gain.Text = "+" .. formatNumber(gain)
			hayUiRows.multiplier.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(1 + hayMultiplierLevelValue * 0.5)
			hayUiRows.cooldown.Text = formatNumber(cooldown) .. "s"
			hayUiRows.amountLvl.Text = tostring(hayAmountLevelValue) .. "/250"
			hayUiRows.multLvl.Text = tostring(hayMultiplierLevelValue) .. "/50"
			hayUiRows.cdLvl.Text = tostring(hayCooldownLevelValue) .. "/25"
			hayUiRows.formula.Text = string.format("(%d + 1) * (1 + %d*0.5)", hayAmountLevelValue, hayMultiplierLevelValue)
		end
		for idx = 1, #HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER do
			local key = HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER[idx]
			local def = getHayUpgradeDefSafe(key)
			local card = getHayUpgradeCard(key)
			if card then
				updateCard(
					card,
					readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, key),
					readHayUpgradeCost(safeHayState, key),
					true,
					def.maxLevel,
					hayCurrencyValue,
					not seventhUnlockedVisual and "Откроется на 7-м перерождении" or nil,
					"Hay"
				)
			end
		end
		if bundle.stats and bundle.stats.luck then
			local effLuck, effSpeed, effBulk = getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
			local speedOverflowBulk = getRuneSpeedOverflowBulk(effSpeed)
			local effBulkBonus = math.max(0, effBulk - 1)
			local speedSeconds = getRuneRollIntervalFromSpeed(effSpeed)
			bundle.stats.luck.Text = formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x"
			bundle.stats.bulk.Text = "+" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
			bundle.stats.speed.Text = string.format("%ss/roll | Overflow Bulk +%s", formatRuneStatValue(speedSeconds), formatRuneStatValue(speedOverflowBulk))
			bundle.stats.total.Text = "Luck " .. formatRuneStatValue(effLuck) .. "x | Speed " .. formatRuneStatValue(effSpeed) .. "x | Bulk +" .. formatRuneStatValue(effBulkBonus)
		end
	end
end

do
	local runeUnlocked = secondUnlockedVisual
	if runeUi.panel and runeUi.panel.Visible and not runeUnlocked then
		runeUi.panel.Visible = false
	end
	if runeUi.sessionPanel then
		runeUi.sessionPanel.Visible = runeUnlocked and runeRollingActive
	end
	local rs = parseRuneState()
	local c = rs.counts or {}
	function stacks(v)
		return math.min(10, tonumber(v) or 0)
	end
	local effLuck, effSpeed, effBulk = getClientEffectiveRuneStats()
	if runeUi.indexText then
		runeUi.indexText.Text = "Трава: " .. formatNumber(c.Grass or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Grass)) .. ")\n"
			.. "Тёмная трава: " .. formatNumber(c.DarkGrass or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.DarkGrass)) .. ")\n"
			.. "Одуванчик: " .. formatNumber(c.Dandelion or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Dandelion)) .. ")\n"
			.. "Цветок: " .. formatNumber(c.Flower or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Flower)) .. ")\n"
			.. "Фиалка: " .. formatNumber(c.Violet or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Violet)) .. ")\n"
			.. "Роза: " .. formatNumber(c.Rose or 0) .. " (эф. " .. formatNumber(stacks(c.Rose)) .. ")\n\n"
			.. "Luck x" .. formatNumber(effLuck) .. " | Speed x" .. formatNumber(effSpeed) .. " | Bulk +" .. formatNumber(math.max(0, effBulk - 1))
	end
	if runeUi.openBtn then
		setButtonVisual(runeUi.openBtn, "ОТКРЫТЬ FOREST RUNE (50 Coins)", coins.Value >= 50 and runeUnlocked, false, Color3.fromRGB(151, 227, 184), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(22, 56, 41), not runeUnlocked)
	end
	if runeUi.luckBtn then runeUi.luckBtn.Text = "Luck (" .. tostring(runeLuckCost.Value) .. " C)" end
	if runeUi.speedBtn then runeUi.speedBtn.Text = "Speed (" .. tostring(runeSpeedCost.Value) .. " W)" end
	if runeUi.bulkBtn then runeUi.bulkBtn.Text = "Bulk (" .. tostring(runeBulkCost.Value) .. " P)" end
	refreshRuneStats()
	local safeHayState = buildStableHaySnapshot()
	local hayAmountLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayAmount")
	local hayMultiplierLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayMultiplier")
	local hayCooldownLevelValue = readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, "HayCooldown")
	local hayCurrencyValue = tonumber(type(safeHayState) == "table" and safeHayState.HayCurrency or 0) or 0
	if hayUiRows.gain then
		local gain = (1 + hayAmountLevelValue) * (1 + hayMultiplierLevelValue * 0.5)
		local cooldown = math.max(0.8, 5 - hayCooldownLevelValue * 0.1)
		hayUiRows.currency.Text = formatNumber(hayCurrencyValue)
		hayUiRows.gain.Text = "+" .. formatNumber(gain)
		hayUiRows.multiplier.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(1 + hayMultiplierLevelValue * 0.5)
		hayUiRows.cooldown.Text = formatNumber(cooldown) .. "s"
		hayUiRows.amountLvl.Text = tostring(hayAmountLevelValue) .. "/250"
		hayUiRows.multLvl.Text = tostring(hayMultiplierLevelValue) .. "/50"
		hayUiRows.cdLvl.Text = tostring(hayCooldownLevelValue) .. "/25"
		hayUiRows.formula.Text = string.format("(%d + 1) * (1 + %d*0.5)", hayAmountLevelValue, hayMultiplierLevelValue)
	end
	for idx = 1, #HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER do
		local key = HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER[idx]
		local def = getHayUpgradeDefSafe(key)
		local card = getHayUpgradeCard(key)
		if card then
			updateCard(
				card,
				readHayUpgradeLevel(safeHayState, key),
				readHayUpgradeCost(safeHayState, key),
				true,
				def.maxLevel,
				hayCurrencyValue,
				not seventhUnlockedVisual and "Откроется на 7-м перерождении" or nil,
				"Hay"
			)
		end
	end
end

if runeUpgradeCards then
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.luck, runeLuckLevel.Value, math.floor(runeLuckCost.Value + 0.5), true, 4, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.speed, runeSpeedLevel.Value, math.floor(runeSpeedCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.bulk, runeBulkLevel.Value, math.floor(runeBulkCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, paperValue.Value, nil, "Paper")
	if runeUpgradeLockedOverlay then
		runeUpgradeLockedOverlay.Visible = false
	end
end

if xpProgressUi then
	local boostValue = 1 + xpBoostLevel.Value
	xpProgressUi.valueText.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(boostValue)
	xpProgressUi.costText.Text = xpBoostNextCost.Value <= 0 and "MAX" or (formatNumber(math.floor(xpBoostNextCost.Value + 0.5)) .. " XP")
	if xpProgressUi.currentText then
		xpProgressUi.currentText.Text = formatNumber(xpValue.Value)
	end
	if xpProgressUi.collectText then
		xpProgressUi.collectText.Text = formatNumber(getClientXpPerCollectEstimate()) .. " XP/sec"
	end
	if xpProgressUi.needText then
		xpProgressUi.needText.Text = xpBoostNextCost.Value <= 0 and "0" or formatNumber(math.max(0, xpBoostNextCost.Value - xpValue.Value))
	end
	if xpProgressUi.multText then
		xpProgressUi.multText.Text = "x" .. formatNumber(1 + xpMultiplierLevel.Value)
	end
	if xpProgressUi.levelText then
		xpProgressUi.levelText.Text = tostring(xpBoostLevel.Value)
	end
	if xpProgressUi.nextUnlockText then
		local nxt = xpBoostLevel.Value < 5 and "Rune XP Tier" or (xpBoostLevel.Value < 10 and "Advanced Rune Tier" or "MAX TIER")
		xpProgressUi.nextUnlockText.Text = nxt
	end
	local progress = xpBoostNextCost.Value > 0 and safeClamp(xpValue.Value / xpBoostNextCost.Value, 0, 1) or 1
	TweenService:Create(xpProgressUi.barFill, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(progress, 0, 1, 0)}):Play()
	if xpProgressUi.barGlow then
		local boost = (xpProgressLastValue and xpValue.Value > xpProgressLastValue) and 0.58 or 0.75
		xpProgressUi.barGlow.BackgroundTransparency = boost
		TweenService:Create(xpProgressUi.barGlow, TweenInfo.new(0.42, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.8}):Play()
	end
	if xpProgressLastValue and xpValue.Value > xpProgressLastValue and xpProgressUi.valueText then
		xpProgressUi.valueText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(170, 255, 230)
		TweenService:Create(xpProgressUi.valueText, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(236, 255, 228)}):Play()
	end
	xpProgressLastValue = xpValue.Value
	setButtonVisual(xpProgressUi.buyButton, "UPGRADE XP BOOST", secondUnlockedVisual and xpValue.Value >= xpBoostNextCost.Value, xpBoostNextCost.Value <= 0, Color3.fromRGB(100, 243, 211), Color3.fromRGB(136, 148, 175), Color3.fromRGB(22, 48, 62), not secondUnlockedVisual)
	if xpProgressLockedOverlay then
		xpProgressLockedOverlay.Visible = false
	end
end


-- Safety pass against stale visual lock states.
if thirdUnlockedVisual then
	updateCard(coinWoodBoostCard, coinWoodBoostLevel.Value, coinWoodBoostCost.Value, coinWoodBoostActive.Value, 10, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
	updateCard(treeCoinBoostCard, woodCoinBoostLevel.Value, woodCoinBoostCost.Value, woodCoinBoostActive.Value, 20, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
end
if secondUnlockedVisual and xpUpgradeCards then
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.coin, coinXpLevel.Value, math.floor(coinXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 10, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.wood, woodXpLevel.Value, math.floor(woodXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 10, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.paper, paperXpLevel.Value, math.floor(paperXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 10, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.xpMul, xpMultiplierLevel.Value, math.floor(xpMultiplierCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.runeLuck, runeLuckXpLevel.Value, math.floor(runeLuckXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 3, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.runeBulk, runeBulkXpLevel.Value, math.floor(runeBulkXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
	updateCard(xpUpgradeCards.runeSpeed, runeSpeedXpLevel.Value, math.floor(runeSpeedXpCost.Value + 0.5), true, 2, xpValue.Value, nil, "XP")
end
if secondUnlockedVisual and runeUpgradeCards then
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.luck, runeLuckLevel.Value, math.floor(runeLuckCost.Value + 0.5), true, 4, coins.Value, nil, "Coins")
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.speed, runeSpeedLevel.Value, math.floor(runeSpeedCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, woodCurrency.Value, nil, "Wood")
	updateCard(runeUpgradeCards.bulk, runeBulkLevel.Value, math.floor(runeBulkCost.Value + 0.5), true, 5, paperValue.Value, nil, "Paper")
end

updateWallVisual()
refreshAdminCurrencyButtons()
updateUnlockDebug()
end

passiveEffectParts = {}
if passiveRollBlock and passiveRollBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, passiveRollBlock)
end
if passiveInventoryBlock and passiveInventoryBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, passiveInventoryBlock)
end
if runeRollBlock and runeRollBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, runeRollBlock)
end
if runeIndexBlock and runeIndexBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, runeIndexBlock)
end
if runeUpgradeBlock and runeUpgradeBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, runeUpgradeBlock)
end
if natureRuneBlock and natureRuneBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, natureRuneBlock)
end
if forestRuneBlock and forestRuneBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, forestRuneBlock)
end
if hayBlock and hayBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
	table.insert(passiveEffectParts, hayBlock)
end
for i = 1, #(passiveEffectParts or {}) do
	(function(p)
		if not p:FindFirstChild("PassiveFxLight") then
			local l = Instance.new("PointLight")
			l.Name = "PassiveFxLight"
			l.Range = 18
			l.Brightness = 2.6
			l.Color = Color3.fromRGB(181, 219, 255)
			l.Parent = p
		end
		if not p:FindFirstChild("PassiveFxHighlight") then
			local h = Instance.new("Highlight")
			h.Name = "PassiveFxHighlight"
			h.Adornee = p
			h.FillColor = (p == hayBlock and Color3.fromRGB(255, 229, 128)) or ((p == runeRollBlock or p == natureRuneBlock) and Color3.fromRGB(122, 255, 220)) or (p == forestRuneBlock and Color3.fromRGB(165, 255, 145)) or Color3.fromRGB(168, 199, 255)
			h.OutlineColor = (p == hayBlock and Color3.fromRGB(255, 247, 196)) or ((p == runeRollBlock or p == natureRuneBlock) and Color3.fromRGB(224, 255, 244)) or (p == forestRuneBlock and Color3.fromRGB(218, 255, 203)) or Color3.fromRGB(245, 249, 255)
			h.FillTransparency = 0.7
			h.OutlineTransparency = 0.02
			h.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
			h.Parent = p
		end
		if not p:FindFirstChild("PassiveFxParticles") then
			local emitter = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
			emitter.Name = "PassiveFxParticles"
			emitter.Rate = 8
			emitter.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.7, 1.2)
			emitter.Speed = NumberRange.new(0.8, 1.8)
			emitter.RotSpeed = NumberRange.new(-30, 30)
			emitter.Size = NumberSequence.new(0.3, 0)
			emitter.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
				NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.35),
				NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
			})
			emitter.Parent = p
		end
	end)(passiveEffectParts[i])
end

function triggerRuneBurst(systemName)
	local target = runeRollBlock
	if systemName == "Forest" and forestRuneBlock and forestRuneBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
		target = forestRuneBlock
	elseif systemName == "Nature" and natureRuneBlock and natureRuneBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
		target = natureRuneBlock
	end
	if not target or not target:IsA("BasePart") then
		return
	end
	local burst = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
	burst.Texture = getAssetOrEmpty(AssetSlots.RuneIcons.Grass)
	if systemName == "Forest" then
		burst.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(176, 121, 76), Color3.fromRGB(97, 73, 45))
	else
		burst.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(122, 255, 116), Color3.fromRGB(66, 184, 82))
	end
	burst.Speed = NumberRange.new(4, 7)
	burst.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.35)
	burst.Rate = 0
	burst.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(360, 360)
	burst.Size = NumberSequence.new({
		NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.35),
		NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0),
	})
	burst.Parent = target
	burst:Emit(14)
	task.delay(0.4, function()
		burst:Destroy()
	end)
end

function triggerHayBurst()
	if not hayBlock or not hayBlock:IsA("BasePart") then return end
	local burst = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
	burst.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(255, 231, 133), Color3.fromRGB(232, 186, 79))
	burst.Speed = NumberRange.new(3, 6)
	burst.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.35)
	burst.Rate = 0
	burst.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(360, 360)
	burst.Size = NumberSequence.new(0.25, 0)
	burst.Parent = hayBlock
	burst:Emit(16)
	task.delay(0.4, function() burst:Destroy() end)
end

function getButtonPurchaseContext(button)
	return {
		button = button,
		text = button and button.Text or "",
		active = button and button.Active or false,
		selectable = button and button.Selectable or false,
	}
end

function checkButtonExistsRequirement(context)
	if context.button then
		return true, "ok"
	end
	return false, "missing_button"
end

function checkButtonInteractableRequirement(context)
	if context.active and context.selectable then
		return true, "ok"
	end
	return false, "inactive"
end

function checkButtonDisplayStateRequirement(context)
	if context.text == "LOCKED" then
		return false, "locked"
	end
	if context.text == "MAX" then
		return false, "maxed"
	end
	return true, "ok"
end

function buildButtonPurchaseState(context)
	local existsOk, existsReason = checkButtonExistsRequirement(context)
	if not existsOk then
		return { purchasable = false, reason = existsReason, displayState = "hidden" }
	end

	local interactableOk, interactableReason = checkButtonInteractableRequirement(context)
	if not interactableOk then
		return { purchasable = false, reason = interactableReason, displayState = "disabled" }
	end

	local displayOk, displayReason = checkButtonDisplayStateRequirement(context)
	if not displayOk then
		return { purchasable = false, reason = displayReason, displayState = displayReason }
	end

	return { purchasable = true, reason = "ok", displayState = "active" }
end

function isButtonPurchasable(button)
	local purchaseState = buildButtonPurchaseState(getButtonPurchaseContext(button))
	return purchaseState.purchasable
end

function bindUpgradeCard(card, family, key)
	if not card then return end
	card.buyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if not isButtonPurchasable(card.buyButton) then return end
		purchaseUpgradeEvent:FireServer(family, key, "Buy")
	end)
	card.maxButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if not isButtonPurchasable(card.maxButton) then return end
		purchaseUpgradeEvent:FireServer(family, key, "Max")
	end)
end

function bindRuneUpgradeCard(card, buyAction, maxAction)
	if not card then return end
	card.buyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if not isButtonPurchasable(card.buyButton) then return end
		runeActionEvent:FireServer(buyAction)
	end)
	card.maxButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if not isButtonPurchasable(card.maxButton) then return end
		runeActionEvent:FireServer(maxAction)
	end)
end
