function bindUpgradeBoards()
	local upgrades = {
		{coinGainCard, "Coin", "CoinValue"},
		{coinMultiCard, "Coin", "Multiplier"},
		{coinSpawnCard, "Coin", "SpawnSpeed"},
		{coinWoodBoostCard, "Coin", "WoodBoost"},
		{treeGainCard, "Wood", "WoodValue"},
		{treeMultiCard, "Wood", "WoodMultiplier"},
		{treeSpeedCard, "Wood", "WoodSpeed"},
		{treeCoinBoostCard, "Wood", "CoinBoost"},
	}
	for i = 1, #upgrades do
		local cfg = upgrades[i]
		bindUpgradeCard(cfg[1], cfg[2], cfg[3])
	end

	if paperUpgradeCards then
		bindUpgradeCard(paperUpgradeCards.gain, "Paper", "PaperValue")
		bindUpgradeCard(paperUpgradeCards.multi, "Paper", "PaperMultiplier")
		bindUpgradeCard(paperUpgradeCards.speed, "Paper", "PaperSpeed")
	end

	if runeUpgradeCards then
		bindRuneUpgradeCard(runeUpgradeCards.luck, "UpgradeLuck", "UpgradeLuckMax")
		bindRuneUpgradeCard(runeUpgradeCards.speed, "UpgradeSpeed", "UpgradeSpeedMax")
		bindRuneUpgradeCard(runeUpgradeCards.bulk, "UpgradeBulk", "UpgradeBulkMax")
	end

	if xpUpgradeCards then
		local xpBindings = {
			{xpUpgradeCards.coin, "CoinXP"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.wood, "WoodXP"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.paper, "PaperXP"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.xpMul, "XPMultiplier"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.runeLuck, "RuneLuckXP"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.runeBulk, "RuneBulkXP"},
			{xpUpgradeCards.runeSpeed, "RuneSpeedXP"},
		}
		for idx = 1, #(xpBindings or {}) do
			local binding = xpBindings[idx]
			bindUpgradeCard(binding[1], "XP", binding[2])
		end
	end
	for idx = 1, #HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER do
		local key = HAY_UPGRADE_ORDER[idx]
		local card = getHayUpgradeCard(key)
		if card then
			bindUpgradeCard(card, "Hay", key)
		end
	end

	if xpProgressUi and xpProgressUi.buyButton then
		xpProgressUi.buyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			xpActionEvent:FireServer("BuyXPBoost")
		end)
	end
end

function bindPassiveAndRuneButtons()
	rebirthButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		purchaseRebirthEvent:FireServer()
		task.delay(0.1, refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
		task.delay(0.5, refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
	end)
	addFuelButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() factoryActionEvent:FireServer("AddFuelOnce") end)
	addFuelMaxButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() factoryActionEvent:FireServer("AddFuelMax") end)

	function firePassiveRoll()
		if isRovRolling then
			showToast("Подожди, ролл уже идет")
			return
		end
		passiveActionEvent:FireServer("Roll")
	end

	if passiveUi.rollButton then passiveUi.rollButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(firePassiveRoll) end
	if passiveUi.rollButtonInventory then passiveUi.rollButtonInventory.MouseButton1Click:Connect(firePassiveRoll) end

	if passiveUi.equipBtn then
		passiveUi.equipBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if passiveUi.selectedUid == "" then
				showToast("Выбери пассив")
				return
			end
			if passiveUi.lastState.equippedUid == passiveUi.selectedUid then
				passiveActionEvent:FireServer("Unequip")
			else
				passiveActionEvent:FireServer("Equip", passiveUi.selectedUid)
			end
		end)
	end

	if passiveUi.deleteBtn then
		passiveUi.deleteBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if passiveUi.selectedUid == "" then
				showToast("Выбери пассив")
				return
			end
			if passiveUi.deleteConfirm then
				passiveUi.deleteConfirm.Visible = true
			end
		end)
	end

	if passiveUi.deleteConfirmYes then
		passiveUi.deleteConfirmYes.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if passiveUi.selectedUid ~= "" then
				passiveActionEvent:FireServer("Delete", passiveUi.selectedUid)
				passiveUi.selectedUid = ""
			end
			passiveUi.deleteConfirm.Visible = false
		end)
	end

	if runeUi.luckBtn then runeUi.luckBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() runeActionEvent:FireServer("UpgradeLuck") end) end
	if runeUi.speedBtn then runeUi.speedBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() runeActionEvent:FireServer("UpgradeSpeed") end) end
	if runeUi.bulkBtn then runeUi.bulkBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() runeActionEvent:FireServer("UpgradeBulk") end) end
end

function bindAdminPanelActions()
	giveCurrencyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		local amount = tonumber(adminAmountBox.Text)
		local targetName = tostring(adminTargetBox.Text or "me")
		if amount then
			adminActionEvent:FireServer("GiveCurrency", selectedAdminCurrency, {amount = amount, targetName = targetName})
		else
			showToast("Введи число")
		end
	end)

	resetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() adminActionEvent:FireServer("ResetSelf") end)
	for _, quickButton in ipairs(adminQuickButtons or {}) do
		quickButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			adminActionEvent:FireServer("GiveCurrency", selectedAdminCurrency, {amount = tonumber(quickButton:GetAttribute("Amount")) or 0, targetName = tostring(adminTargetBox.Text or "me")})
		end)
	end

	givePassiveButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		local passiveId = tostring(adminPassiveBox.Text or "")
		if passiveId == "" then
			showToast("Укажи passive id")
			return
		end
		adminActionEvent:FireServer("GivePassive", passiveId, {targetName = tostring(adminTargetBox.Text or "me")})
	end)

	adminRuneBoostButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		adminActionEvent:FireServer("AdminRuneBoost", "", {targetName = tostring(adminTargetBox.Text or "me")})
	end)

	startAllEventsButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		adminActionEvent:FireServer("StartServerEvent", "All", selectedAdminDuration)
	end)

	duration5Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() selectedAdminDuration = 300 end)
	duration15Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() selectedAdminDuration = 900 end)
	duration60Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() selectedAdminDuration = 3600 end)

	for eventId in pairs(eventButtons) do
		eventButtons[eventId].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			selectedAdminEvent = eventId
			adminActionEvent:FireServer("StartServerEvent", selectedAdminEvent, selectedAdminDuration)
		end)
	end

	toggleAdminButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		adminFrame.Visible = not adminFrame.Visible
		toggleAdminButton.Text = adminFrame.Visible and "Admin Hide" or "Admin Show"
	end)
end

function registerNotifyEventListeners()
	notifyEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(payload)
		if typeof(payload) ~= "table" then
			showToast(tostring(payload))
			return
		end

		if payload.kind == "pickup" then
			local ok = pcall(function()
				showPickup(payload.icon or "Coin", payload.amount or 0)
			end)
			if tostring(payload.icon or "") == "Hay" then
				triggerHayBurst()
			end
			if not ok then
				showToast("+" .. tostring(payload.amount or 0))
			end
		elseif payload.kind == "passive_roll_result" then
			local def = PASSIVE_DEFS[payload.passiveId or ""]
			if def then
				playRovAnimation(def)
				showToast("Новый пассив: " .. def.name .. " [" .. def.rarity .. "]")
			else
				showToast("Пассив получен")
			end
		elseif payload.kind == "rune_roll_result" then
			local rolled = payload.rolled or {}
			showToast("Открыто рун: " .. tostring(#(rolled or {})))
		elseif payload.kind == "rune_roll_state" then
			local systemName = tostring(rawget(payload, "system") or "Nature")
			if systemName ~= "Nature" and systemName ~= "Forest" then
				return
			end
			if payload.active then startRuneRolling(systemName) else stopRuneRolling(systemName) end
		elseif payload.kind == "rune_roll_tick" then
			local systemName = tostring(rawget(payload, "system") or "Nature")
			if systemName ~= "Nature" and systemName ~= "Forest" then
				return
			end
			local session = payload.session or {}
			effectiveRuneDenominators = payload.effectiveDenominators or effectiveRuneDenominators
			if not runeRollingActive or activeRuneSystem ~= systemName then startRuneRolling(systemName) end
			updateRuneSession(systemName, session)
			refreshRuneStats()
			triggerRuneBurst(systemName)
		elseif payload.kind == "admin_event_state" then
			activeAdminEvents = normalizeAdminEvents(payload.events)
			renderAdminEvents(activeAdminEvents)
			if updateBoards then updateBoards() end
		else
			showToast(payload.text or "Готово")
		end
	end)
end

function registerWorldInputBindings()
	mouse.Button1Down:Connect(function()
		if UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() then return end

		if not isSystemUnlocked(2) then
			if passiveUi.indexPanel and mouse.Target == passiveRollBlock then
				passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible = not passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible
			elseif passiveUi.inventoryPanel and mouse.Target == passiveInventoryBlock then
				passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible = not passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible
			end
			return
		end

		if mouse.Target == treeBlock then
			woodClickEvent:FireServer()
			return
		end

		if passiveUi.indexPanel and mouse.Target == passiveRollBlock then
			if isSystemUnlocked(5) then
				passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible = false
				passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible = not passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible
			else
				showToast("Пассивы откроются на 5-м перерождении")
			end
			return
		end

		if passiveUi.inventoryPanel and mouse.Target == passiveInventoryBlock then
			if isSystemUnlocked(5) then
				passiveUi.indexPanel.Visible = false
				passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible = not passiveUi.inventoryPanel.Visible
			else
				showToast("Пассивы откроются на 5-м перерождении")
			end
			return
		end

		if mouse.Target == runeRollBlock or mouse.Target == runeIndexBlock then
			if not isSystemUnlocked(6) then
				showToast("Руны откроются на 6-м перерождении")
			end
			return
		end
	end)
end

function registerWatchedValueUpdates()
	local watchedValues = {
		coins,
		coinValueLevel, coinMultiplierLevel, coinSpawnLevel, coinWoodBoostLevel,
		coinValueCost, coinMultiplierCost, coinSpawnCost, coinWoodBoostCost,
		coinValueActive, coinMultiplierActive, coinSpawnActive, coinWoodBoostActive,
		woodCurrency,
		woodValueLevel, woodMultiplierLevel, woodSpeedLevel, woodCoinBoostLevel,
		woodValueCost, woodMultiplierCost, woodSpeedCost, woodCoinBoostCost,
		woodValueActive, woodMultiplierActive, woodSpeedActive, woodCoinBoostActive,
		paperValue, fuelValue, factoryCountdown, factoryRunning,
		paperValueLevel, paperMultiplierLevel, paperSpeedLevel,
		paperValueCost, paperMultiplierCost, paperSpeedCost,
		paperValueActive, paperMultiplierActive, paperSpeedActive,
		rebirthCount, rebirthNextCost, rebirthNextCurrency,
		rebirthCoinMultiplierBonus, rebirthSpawnSpeedBonus, rebirthWoodMultiplierBonus,
		secondAreaUnlocked, thirdUpgradeUnlocked, fourthSystemsUnlocked, fifthSystemsUnlocked, sixthSystemsUnlocked,
		passiveStateJson, runeStateJson, runeLuckLevel, runeSpeedLevel, runeBulkLevel, runeLuckCost, runeSpeedCost, runeBulkCost,
		doubleCoinsGamepass, doublePaperGamepass, doubleWoodGamepass, tripleRuneLuckGamepass,
		xpValue, coinXpLevel, woodXpLevel, paperXpLevel, xpMultiplierLevel, runeLuckXpLevel, runeBulkXpLevel, runeSpeedXpLevel,
		coinXpCost, woodXpCost, paperXpCost, xpMultiplierCost, runeLuckXpCost, runeBulkXpCost, runeSpeedXpCost, xpBoostLevel, xpBoostNextCost,
	}
	for i = 1, #(watchedValues or {}) do
		local watched = watchedValues[i]
		if watched then watched:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(updateBoards) end
	end
end

function refreshClientUnlockVisibility()
	if updateBoards then
		updateBoards()
	end
end

function startRuntimeUiUpdates()
	if passiveUi.hintEmoji then
		RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			local t = os.clock()
			local blink = math.sin(t * 1.2)
			if blink > 0.985 then
				passiveUi.hintEmoji.Text = ";)"
			elseif blink < -0.985 then
				passiveUi.hintEmoji.Text = "-_-"
			else
				passiveUi.hintEmoji.Text = "😊"
			end
			passiveUi.hintEmoji.Rotation = math.sin(t * 0.8) * 6
			if runeRollBlock and runeRollBlock:IsA("BasePart") then
				local pulse = (math.sin(t * 1.6) + 1) * 0.5
				local green = math.floor(120 + pulse * 90)
				runeRollBlock.Color = Color3.fromRGB(40 + math.floor(pulse * 24), green, 52 + math.floor(pulse * 24))
				local light = runeRollBlock:FindFirstChild("PassiveFxLight")
				if light and light:IsA("PointLight") then
					light.Brightness = 1.5 + pulse * 1.2
					light.Color = Color3.fromRGB(122, 255, 138)
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	function tickAdminEventTimers()
		if type(activeAdminEvents) ~= "table" or #activeAdminEvents == 0 then return end
		local nextEvents = {}
		for idx = 1, #activeAdminEvents do
			local ev = activeAdminEvents[idx]
			local eventData = type(ev) == "table" and ev or {}
			local left = math.max(0, (tonumber(eventData.timeLeft) or 0) - 1)
			eventData.timeLeft = left
			if left > 0 then nextEvents[#nextEvents + 1] = ev end
		end
		activeAdminEvents = nextEvents
		renderAdminEvents(activeAdminEvents)
	end

	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			task.wait(1)
			tickAdminEventTimers()
		end
	end)

	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			task.wait(0.2)
			updateBoards()
		end
	end)

	if #(passiveEffectParts or {}) > 0 then
		RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			local t = os.clock()
			for idx, part in ipairs(passiveEffectParts) do
				local alpha = (math.sin(t * (1.3 + idx * 0.2)) + 1) / 2
				part.Color = Color3.fromRGB(95 + math.floor(alpha * 90), 130 + math.floor(alpha * 70), 210 + math.floor(alpha * 45))
				local light = part:FindFirstChild("PassiveFxLight")
				if light then light.Brightness = 1.2 + alpha * 2.1 end
			end
		end)
	end
end

function initializeClientBindingsAndRuntime()
	bindAdminCurrencySelectors()
	bindUpgradeBoards()
	bindPassiveAndRuneButtons()
	bindAdminPanelActions()
	registerNotifyEventListeners()
	registerWorldInputBindings()
	registerWatchedValueUpdates()
	rebirthCount:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
	secondAreaUnlocked:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
	fourthSystemsUnlocked:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
	sixthSystemsUnlocked:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(refreshClientUnlockVisibility)
	startRuntimeUiUpdates()
end

initializeClientBindingsAndRuntime()
refreshClientUnlockVisibility()
